**File: `src/server/actions/auth.ts`**
```typescript
"use server";

import { createServerAction, ZSAError } from "zsa";
import { z } from "zod";
import { 
  createAndStoreSession, 
  canSignUp, 
  getUserFromDB, 
  generateSessionToken,
  setSessionTokenCookie,
  clearSession,
  requireAdmin,
  getUserTeamsWithPermissions
} from "@/utils/auth";
import { sendVerificationEmail } from "@/utils/email";
import { kv } from "@/lib/kv";
import { getVerificationTokenKey } from "@/utils/auth-utils";
import { generatePasskeyRegistrationOptions } from "@/utils/webauthn";
import { userTable, teamInvitationTable } from "@/db/schema";
import { eq } from "drizzle-orm";
import { db } from "@/db";

// Input Schemas derived from atlas variations
const signUpSchema = z.object({
  email: z.string().email(),
  firstName: z.string().min(2, "First name must be at least 2 characters").max(50),
  lastName: z.string().min(2, "Last name must be at least 2 characters").max(50),
  password: z.string().min(8, "Password must be at least 8 characters"),
  captchaToken: z.string(), // catchaSchema reference from metadata
});

const signInSchema = z.object({
  email: z.string().email(),
  password: z.string().min(8),
  captchaToken: z.string(),
});

const verifyEmailSchema = z.object({
  token: z.string(),
});

const resetPasswordSchema = z.object({
  token: z.string(),
  password: z.string().min(8),
  confirmPassword: z.string(),
});

const updateProfileSchema = z.object({
  firstName: z.string().min(2).max(50),
  lastName: z.string().min(2).max(50),
});

// Server Action: Sign Up
export const signUpAction = createServerAction()
  .input(signUpSchema)
  .handler(async ({ input }) => {
    // Validate signup eligibility
    await canSignUp({ email: input.email });
    
    // Check if user exists
    const existingUser = await getUserFromDB(input.email);
    if (existingUser) {
      throw new ZSAError("CONFLICT", "User already exists");
    }
    
    // Create user logic (implied by metadata)
    const userId = generateSessionToken(); // Using token gen for ID example
    
    // Create session
    await createAndStoreSession(userId, "password");
    
    // Send verification email
    const verificationToken = generateSessionToken();
    await sendVerificationEmail({
      email: input.email,
      verificationToken,
      username: `${input.firstName} ${input.lastName}`,
    });
    
    // Store verification token in KV
    await kv.put(
      getVerificationTokenKey(input.email), 
      verificationToken, 
      { expirationTtl: Math.floor(24 * 60 * 60) } // 24 hours
    );
    
    return { success: true, userId };
  });

// Server Action: Sign In
export const signInAction = createServerAction()
  .input(signInSchema)
  .handler(async ({ input }) => {
    const user = await getUserFromDB(input.email);
    if (!user) {
      throw new ZSAError("NOT_FOUND", "Invalid credentials");
    }
    
    // Password verification logic (implied)
    // ...
    
    await createAndStoreSession(user.id, "password");
    
    return { success: true, user };
  });

// Server Action: Verify Email
export const verifyEmailAction = createServerAction()
  .input(verifyEmailSchema)
  .handler(async ({ input }) => {
    // Verification logic using KV
    const storedToken = await kv.get(`verification:${input.token}`);
    if (!storedToken) {
      throw new ZSAError("INVALID_TOKEN", "Token expired or invalid");
    }
    
    // Update user emailVerified status
    // ...
    
    return { success: true };
  });

// Server Action: Reset Password
export const resetPasswordAction = createServerAction()
  .input(resetPasswordSchema)
  .handler(async ({ input }) => {
    if (input.password !== input.confirmPassword) {
      throw new ZSAError("VALIDATION_ERROR", "Passwords do not match");
    }
    
    // Token validation and password update logic
    // ...
    
    return { success: true };
  });

// Server Action: Update Profile
export const updateProfileAction = createServerAction()
  .input(updateProfileSchema)
  .handler(async ({ input }) => {
    // Session validation implied
    // Update user in DB
    return { success: true };
  });

// Server Action: Sign Out
export const signOutAction = createServerAction()
  .handler(async () => {
    await clearSession();
    return { success: true };
  });
```

**File: `src/server/actions/team.ts`**
```typescript
"use server";

import { createServerAction, ZSAError } from "zsa";
import { z } from "zod";
import { db } from "@/db";
import { teamInvitationTable } from "@/db/schema";
import { requireAdmin, getUserTeamsWithPermissions } from "@/utils/auth";

const createTeamSchema = z.object({
  name: z.string().min(1, "Team name is required").max(100),
  description: z.string().max(1000, "Description is too long").optional(),
  avatarUrl: z.string().url("Invalid URL").max(600, "URL is too long").optional().or(z.literal("")),
});

const inviteUserSchema = z.object({
  teamId: z.string().min(1),
  email: z.string().email("Invalid email").max(255),
  roleId: z.string().min(1),
  isSystemRole: z.boolean().optional().default(false),
});

const switchTeamSchema = z.object({
  selectedTeam: z.string().optional(),
});

export const createTeamAction = createServerAction()
  .input(createTeamSchema)
  .handler(async ({ input }) => {
    // Create team logic
    // ...
    return { success: true, teamId: "generated-id" };
  });

export const inviteUserAction = createServerAction()
  .input(inviteUserSchema)
  .handler(async ({ input }) => {
    // Check permissions
    const teams = await getUserTeamsWithPermissions(input.teamId);
    const hasPermission = teams.some(t => t.id === input.teamId);
    
    if (!hasPermission) {
      throw new ZSAError("FORBIDDEN", "Insufficient permissions");
    }
    
    // Create invitation
    await db.insert(teamInvitationTable).values({
      email: input.email,
      teamId: input.teamId,
      roleId: input.roleId,
    });
    
    return { success: true };
  });

export const switchTeamAction = createServerAction()
  .input(switchTeamSchema)
  .handler(async ({ input }) => {
    // Switch team logic
    return { success: true };
  });
```

**File: `src/server/actions/passkey.ts`**
```typescript
"use server";

import { createServerAction, ZSAError } from "zsa";
import { z } from "zod";
import { generatePasskeyRegistrationOptions } from "@/utils/webauthn";

const passkeyRegistrationSchema = z.object({
  response: z.custom(), // WebAuthn response
  challenge: z.string(),
});

const passkeyAuthSchema = z.object({
  response: z.custom(),
  challenge: z.string(),
});

const credentialIdSchema = z.object({
  credentialId: z.string(),
});

export const verifyPasskeyRegistrationAction = createServerAction()
  .input(passkeyRegistrationSchema)
  .handler(async ({ input }) => {
    // Verification logic
    const verification = { verified: true, registrationInfo: {} };
    
    if (!verification.verified) {
      throw new ZSAError("VERIFICATION_FAILED", "Passkey verification failed");
    }
    
    return { success: true };
  });

export const verifyPasskeyAuthenticationAction = createServerAction()
  .input(passkeyAuthSchema)
  .handler(async ({ input }) => {
    // Authentication verification
    return { success: true };
  });

export const registerPasskeyAction = createServerAction()
  .input(credentialIdSchema)
  .handler(async ({ input }) => {
    // Register passkey logic
    return { success: true };
  });

export const removePasskeyAction = createServerAction()
  .input(credentialIdSchema)
  .handler(async ({ input }) => {
    // Remove passkey logic
    return { success: true };
  });

export const getPasskeyRegistrationOptionsAction = createServerAction()
  .handler(async () => {
    const options = await generatePasskeyRegistrationOptions("userId", "email");
    return { options };
  });
```

**File: `src/components/forms/sign-up-form.tsx`**
```typescript
"use client";

import { useServerAction } from "zsa-react";
import { signUpAction } from "@/server/actions/auth";
import { toast } from "sonner";
import { useRouter } from "next/navigation";
import { useForm } from "react-hook-form";
import { zodResolver } from "@hookform/resolvers/zod";
import { z } from "zod";

const formSchema = z.object({
  email: z.string().email(),
  firstName: z.string().min(2),
  lastName: z.string().min(2),
  password: z.string().min(8),
  captchaToken: z.string(),
});

export function SignUpForm() {
  const router = useRouter();
  
  const form = useForm<z.infer<typeof formSchema>>({
    resolver: zodResolver(formSchema),
    defaultValues: {
      email: "",
      firstName: "",
      lastName: "",
      password: "",
      captchaToken: "",
    },
  });

  const { execute: executeSignUp, isPending } = useServerAction(signUpAction, {
    onError: (error) => {
      toast.error(error.message);
    },
    onSuccess: () => {
      toast.success("Account created successfully! Please verify your email.");
      router.push("/auth/verify-email");
    },
  });

  async function onSubmit(values: z.infer<typeof formSchema>) {
    await executeSignUp(values);
  }

  return (
    <form onSubmit={form.handleSubmit(onSubmit)}>
      {/* Form fields implementation */}
    </form>
  );
}
```

**File: `src/components/team/team-switcher.tsx`**
```typescript
"use client";

import { useServerAction } from "zsa-react";
import { switchTeamAction } from "@/server/actions/team";
import { toast } from "sonner";
import { useRouter } from "next/navigation";

export function TeamSwitcher() {
  const router = useRouter();
  
  const { execute: switchTeam, isPending } = useServerAction(switchTeamAction, {
    onError: (error) => {
      toast.error(error.err.message || "Failed to switch team");
    },
    onSuccess: () => {
      toast.success("Team switched");
      router.refresh();
    },
  });

  return (
    <button onClick={() => switchTeam({ selectedTeam: "team-id" })}>
      Switch Team
    </button>
  );
}
```

**File: `src/components/workflow/workflow-editor.tsx`**
```typescript
"use client";

import { useServerAction } from "zsa-react";
import { saveWorkflowAction } from "@/server/actions/workflow";
import { toast } from "sonner";
import { useReactFlow } from "@xyflow/react";

export function WorkflowEditor({ workflowId }: { workflowId: string }) {
  const { getNodes, getEdges } = useReactFlow();
  
  const { execute: saveWorkflow, isPending } = useServerAction(saveWorkflowAction, {
    onError: (error) => {
      toast.error(error.message);
    },
    onStart: () => {
      toast.loading("Saving workflow...");
    },
    onSuccess: () => {
      toast.dismiss();
      toast.success("Workflow saved");
    },
  });

  async function handleSave() {
    const graphJson = JSON.stringify({
      nodes: getNodes(),
      edges: getEdges(),
    });
    
    await saveWorkflow({ workflowId, graphJson });
  }

  return <button onClick={handleSave}>Save</button>;
}
```

### A) RECONSTRUCTED CODE

Based on the atlas metadata, the following Drizzle ORM with SQLite patterns are reconstructed:

**File: `src/db/schema.ts`**

```typescript
import { sqliteTable, text, integer, index } from "drizzle-orm/sqlite-core";
import { relations, InferSelectModel, eq, and, or, gt, lt, desc, asc, count, sql, isNull } from "drizzle-orm";

// Common ID generation pattern observed
const createId = () => crypto.randomUUID(); // VOCAB_MISSING: actual createId implementation

// Table: users
export const users = sqliteTable("users", {
  id: text().primaryKey().$defaultFn(() => `usr_${createId()}`).notNull(),
  firstName: text(),
  lastName: text(),
  email: text({ length: 255 }).unique(),
  passwordHash: text(),
  role: text({ enum: ["USER", "ADMIN"] }).default("USER").notNull(), // VOCAB_MISSING: actual roleTuple
  emailVerified: integer(),
  signUpIpAddress: text(),
  googleAccountId: text(),
  avatar: text(),
  currentCredits: integer().default(0).notNull(),
  lastCreditRefreshAt: integer(),
});

// Table: passkeys
export const passkeys = sqliteTable("passkeys", {
  id: text().primaryKey().$defaultFn(() => `pkey_${createId()}`).notNull(),
  userId: text().notNull().references(() => users.id),
  credentialId: text({ length: 255 }).notNull().unique(),
  credentialPublicKey: text({ length: 255 }).notNull(),
  counter: integer().notNull(),
  transports: text(),
  aaguid: text(),
  userAgent: text(),
  ipAddress: text(),
});

// Table: creditTransactions
export const creditTransactions = sqliteTable("creditTransactions", {
  id: text().primaryKey().$defaultFn(() => `ctxn_${createId()}`).notNull(),
  userId: text().notNull().references(() => users.id),
  amount: integer().notNull(),
  remainingAmount: integer().default(0).notNull(),
  type: text({ enum: ["PURCHASE", "REFUND", "BONUS"] }).notNull(), // VOCAB_MISSING: actual creditTransactionTypeTuple
  description: text({ length: 255 }).notNull(),
  expirationDate: integer(),
  expirationDateProcessedAt: integer(),
  paymentIntentId: text(),
});

// Table: purchasedItems
export const purchasedItems = sqliteTable("purchasedItems", {
  id: text().primaryKey().$defaultFn(() => `pitem_${createId()}`).notNull(),
```

**File: `src/db/queries.ts` (Query Patterns)**
```typescript
import { eq, and, sql } from "drizzle-orm";
import { getDB } from "@/db";
import { 
  userTable, 
  creditTransactionTable, 
  teamTable, 
  teamMembershipTable,
  teamInvitationTable,
  projectTable,
  passKeyCredentialTable
} from "@/db/schema";

// Query Pattern: findFirst with where clause
export async function getUserById(id: string) {
  const db = getDB();
  return db.query.userTable.findFirst({
    where: eq(userTable.id, id),
  });
}

// Query Pattern: findFirst with columns selection
export async function getUserByEmail(email: string) {
  const db = getDB();
  return db.query.userTable.findFirst({
    where: eq(userTable.email, email),
    columns: { id: true, email: true, passwordHash: true },
  });
}

// Query Pattern: findMany with where, orderBy, limit, offset
export async function getCreditTransactions(userId: string, limit: number, offset: number) {
  const db = getDB();
  return db.query.creditTransactionTable.findMany({
    where: eq(creditTransactionTable.userId, userId),
    orderBy: [desc(creditTransactionTable.createdAt)],
    limit,
    offset,
  });
}

// Query Pattern: findMany with and() where clause
export async function getTeamMemberships(teamId: string, userId: string) {
  const db = getDB();
  return db.query.teamMembershipTable.findMany({
    where: and(
      eq(teamMembershipTable.teamId, teamId),
      eq(teamMembershipTable.userId, userId)
    ),
  });
}

// Query Pattern: findFirst with relations (with)
export async function getTeamWithMembers(teamId: string) {
  const db = getDB();
  return db.query.teamTable.findFirst({
    where: eq(teamTable.id, teamId),
    with: {
      members: true,
    },
  });
}
```

**File: `src/db/mutations.ts` (Mutation Patterns)**
```typescript
import { eq, sql } from "drizzle-orm";
import { getDB } from "@/db";
import { userTable, creditTransactionTable, teamTable, teamMembershipTable } from "@/db/schema";

// Insert Pattern: values with returning
export async function createUser(data: typeof userTable.$inferInsert) {
  const db = getDB();
  const [user] = await db.insert(userTable)
    .values({
      email: data.email,
      firstName: data.firstName,
      lastName: data.lastName,
      passwordHash: data.passwordHash,
      signUpIpAddress: data.signUpIpAddress,
      currentCredits: 0,
      emailVerified: false,
      createdAt: new Date(),
    })
    .returning();
  return user;
}

// Update Pattern: set with where and returning
export async function updateUserCredits(userId: string, newCredits: number) {
  const db = getDB();
  const [updatedUser] = await db.update(userTable)
    .set({ currentCredits: newCredits, lastCreditRefreshAt: new Date() })
    .where(eq(userTable.id, userId))
    .returning();
  return updatedUser;
}

// Update Pattern: set with sql expression
export async function decrementCredits(userId: string, amount: number) {
  const db = getDB();
  return db.update(userTable)
    .set({ 
      currentCredits: sql`${userTable.currentCredits} - ${amount}` 
    })
    .where(eq(userTable.id, userId));
}

// Delete Pattern: where clause
export async function deleteTeamInvitation(invitationId: string) {
  const db = getDB();
  return db.delete(teamInvitationTable)
    .where(eq(teamInvitationTable.id, invitationId));
}
```

```typescript
export async function getTeamById(teamId: string) {
  // Reconstructed from: Declaration::teamTable.id::CALL metadata

    where: eq(teamTable.id, teamId),
  });

}

// Pattern 3: Query with findMany and relations
export async function getUserTeamsAction(userId: string) {
  // Reconstructed from: Declaration::getUserTeamsAction::CONST metadata
  const memberships = await db.query.teamMembershipTable.findMany({
    where: eq(teamMembershipTable.userId, userId),
    with: {
      team: true,
    },
  });
  return memberships;
}

// Pattern 4: Mutation with insert
export async function createTeamAction(input: { name: string; slug: string }) {
  // Reconstructed from: Declaration::createTeamAction::CONST metadata

  await db.insert(teamTable).values({
    id,
    name: input.name,
    slug: input.slug,
    createdAt: new Date(),
    updatedAt: new Date(),
  });
  return { id };
}

// Pattern 4: Mutation with update
export async function updateTeamAction(teamId: string, input: { name: string }) {
  await db.update(teamTable)
    .set({ 
      name: input.name, 
      updatedAt: new Date() 
    })
    .where(eq(teamTable.id, teamId));
}

// Pattern 4: Mutation with delete
export async function deleteTeamAction(teamId: string) {
  await db.delete(teamTable)
    .where(eq(teamTable.id, teamId));
}
```

```typescript
// Teams Table (inferred from teamRoleRelations and actions)
export const teams = sqliteTable('teams', {
  id: text('id').primaryKey().notNull(),
  name: text('name').notNull(),
  slug: text('slug').unique().notNull(),
  createdAt: integer('created_at', { mode: 'timestamp' }).notNull(),
  updatedAt: integer('updated_at', { mode: 'timestamp' }).notNull(),
});

// Team Roles Table (referenced in teamRoleRelations)
export const teamRoles = sqliteTable('team_roles', {
  id: text('id').primaryKey().notNull(),
  teamId: text('team_id').notNull().references(() => teams.id),
  userId: text('user_id').notNull(),
  roleId: text('role_id').notNull(),
  isSystemRole: integer('is_system_role', { mode: 'boolean' }).notNull(),
  createdAt: integer('created_at', { mode: 'timestamp' }).notNull(),
});

// Projects Table (referenced in projectRelations and getUserProjectsAction)
export const projects = sqliteTable('projects', {
  id: text('id').primaryKey().notNull(),
  teamId: text('team_id').notNull().references(() => teams.id),
  name: text('name').notNull(),
  description: text('description'),
  createdAt: integer('created_at', { mode: 'timestamp' }).notNull(),
  updatedAt: integer('updated_at', { mode: 'timestamp' }).notNull(),
});

  graph: text('graph', { mode: 'json' }).notNull(), // JSON stored as text

  updatedAt: integer('updated_at', { mode: 'timestamp' }).notNull(),
});

export const users = sqliteTable('users', {
  id: text('id').primaryKey().notNull(),
  email: text('email').unique().notNull(),
  firstName: text('first_name'),
  lastName: text('last_name'),
  password: text('password'), // hashed
  emailVerified: integer('email_verified', { mode: 'boolean' }).notNull().default(0),
  createdAt: integer('created_at', { mode: 'timestamp' }).notNull(),
  updatedAt: integer('updated_at', { mode: 'timestamp' }).notNull(),
});

// Sessions Table (referenced in getSessionsAction, deleteSessionAction)
export const sessions = sqliteTable('sessions', {
  id: text('id').primaryKey().notNull(),
  userId: text('user_id').notNull().references(() => users.id),
  token: text('token').unique().notNull(),
  expiresAt: integer('expires_at', { mode: 'timestamp' }).notNull(),
  createdAt: integer('created_at', { mode: 'timestamp' }).notNull(),
});

// Team Invites Table (referenced in teamInviteSchema, acceptTeamInviteAction)

  teamId: text('team_id').notNull().references(() => teams.id),
  email: text('email').notNull(),
  roleId: text('role_id').notNull(),
  token: text('token').unique().notNull(),

});

  id: text('id').primaryKey().notNull(),

});

// RELATIONS DEFINITIONS (Visible in atlas as CONST declarations)
export const teamRelations = relations(teams, ({ many }) => ({
  members: many(teamRoles),
  projects: many(projects),
  invites: many(teamInvites),
}));

export const teamRoleRelations = relations(teamRoles, ({ one }) => ({
  team: one(teams, {
    fields: [teamRoles.teamId],
    references: [teams.id],
  }),
  user: one(users, {
    fields: [teamRoles.userId],
    references: [users.id],
  }),
}));

export const projectRelations = relations(projects, ({ one, many }) => ({
  team: one(teams, {
    fields: [projects.teamId],
    references: [teams.id],
  }),
  workflows: many(workflows),
}));

export const workflowRelations = relations(workflows, ({ one }) => ({
  project: one(projects, {
    fields: [workflows.projectId],
    references: [projects.id],
  }),
}));

export const userRelations = relations(users, ({ many }) => ({
  sessions: many(sessions),
  teamRoles: many(teamRoles),
  passkeys: many(passkeys),
}));

// TYPE INFERENCE PATTERNS
export type Team = InferSelectModel<typeof teams>;
export type NewTeam = InferInsertModel<typeof teams>;
export type User = InferSelectModel<typeof users>;
export type NewUser = InferInsertModel<typeof users>;
```

```typescript
import { drizzle } from 'drizzle-orm/libsql';
import { createClient } from '@libsql/client';
import * as schema from './schema';

// Database client configuration
const client = createClient({
  url: process.env.DATABASE_URL || 'file:./local.db',
  authToken: process.env.DATABASE_AUTH_TOKEN,
});

// Database instance with schema
export const db = drizzle(client, { schema });
```

**File: `src/app/actions/teams.ts` (Server Actions - Query Patterns)**
```typescript
'use server';

import { db } from '@/db';
import { teams, teamRoles, teamInvites, users } from '@/db/schema';
import { eq, and, desc, asc } from 'drizzle-orm';
import { revalidatePath } from 'next/cache';

// QUERY PATTERN: db.query.tableName.findFirst with where clause
export const getUserProjectsAction = async (userId: string) => {
  const userWithTeams = await db.query.users.findFirst({
    where: eq(users.id, userId),
    with: {
      teamRoles: {
        with: {
          team: {
            with: {
              projects: true,
            },
          },
        },
      },
    },
  });
  
  return userWithTeams?.teamRoles.flatMap(tr => tr.team.projects) || [];
};

// QUERY PATTERN: db.query.tableName.findMany with where and order
export const getPendingInvitationsForCurrentUserAction = async (email: string) => {
  const invitations = await db.query.teamInvites.findMany({
    where: and(
      eq(teamInvites.email, email),
      eq(teamInvites.expiresAt, new Date()) // gt check would be here
    ),
    with: {
      team: true,
    },
    orderBy: desc(teamInvites.createdAt),
  });
  
  return invitations;
};

// QUERY PATTERN: db.query with nested relations
export const getSessionsAction = async (userId: string) => {
  const userSessions = await db.query.sessions.findMany({
    where: eq(sessions.userId, userId),
    orderBy: desc(sessions.createdAt),
  });
  
  return userSessions;
};
```

**File: `src/app/actions/projects.ts` (Server Actions - Mutation Patterns)**
```typescript
'use server';

import { db } from '@/db';
import { projects, workflows, teams } from '@/db/schema';
import { eq, and } from 'drizzle-orm';
import { revalidatePath } from 'next/cache';
import { generateId } from '@/lib/utils';

// MUTATION PATTERN: db.insert.values
export const createProjectAction = async (input: { 
  teamId: string; 
  name: string; 
  description?: string 
}) => {
  const id = generateId();
  
  await db.insert(projects).values({
    id,
    teamId: input.teamId,
    name: input.name,
    description: input.description || null,
    createdAt: new Date(),
    updatedAt: new Date(),
  });
  
  revalidatePath(`/dashboard/${input.teamId}`);
  return { id };
};

// MUTATION PATTERN: db.update.set.where
export const updateUserProfileAction = async (userId: string, input: {
  firstName?: string;
  lastName?: string;
}) => {
  await db.update(users)
    .set({
      firstName: input.firstName,
      lastName: input.lastName,
      updatedAt: new Date(),
    })
    .where(eq(users.id, userId));
    
  revalidatePath('/dashboard/settings');
};

// MUTATION PATTERN: db.delete.where
export const deleteSessionAction = async (sessionId: string) => {
  await db.delete(sessions)
    .where(eq(sessions.id, sessionId));
};

export const removeTeamMemberAction = async (teamId: string, userId: string) => {
  await db.delete(teamRoles)
    .where(
      and(
        eq(teamRoles.teamId, teamId),
        eq(teamRoles.userId, userId)
      )
    );
    
  revalidatePath(`/dashboard/${teamId}/members`);
};

// COMPLEX MUTATION: Transaction-like operations
export const acceptTeamInviteAction = async (input: {
  token: string;
  userId: string;
}) => {
  // First find the invite
  const invite = await db.query.teamInvites.findFirst({
    where: eq(teamInvites.token, input.token),
  });
  
  if (!invite) throw new Error('Invalid token');
  
  // Add user to team
  await db.insert(teamRoles).values({
    id: generateId(),
    teamId: invite.teamId,
    userId: input.userId,
    roleId: invite.roleId,
    isSystemRole: false,
    createdAt: new Date(),
  });
  
  // Delete the invite
  await db.delete(teamInvites)
    .where(eq(teamInvites.id, invite.id));
    
  revalidatePath('/dashboard');
};
```

**File: `src/app/actions/workflows.ts` (Workflow Operations)**
```typescript
'use server';

import { db } from '@/db';
import { workflows } from '@/db/schema';
import { eq } from 'drizzle-orm';

export const getProjectWorkflowsAction = async (projectId: string) => {
  return await db.query.workflows.findMany({
    where: eq(workflows.projectId, projectId),
    orderBy: desc(workflows.updatedAt),
  });
};

export const getWorkflowAction = async (id: string) => {
  return await db.query.workflows.findFirst({
    where: eq(workflows.id, id),
  });
};

export const saveWorkflowAction = async (input: {
  id?: string;
  projectId: string;
  name: string;
  graph: any; // JSON structure
}) => {
  if (input.id) {
    // Update existing
    await db.update(workflows)
      .set({
        name: input.name,
        graph: JSON.stringify(input.graph),
        updatedAt: new Date(),
      })
      .where(eq(workflows.id, input.id));
      
    return { id: input.id };
  } else {
    // Create new
    const id = generateId();
    await db.insert(workflows).values({
      id,
      projectId: input.projectId,
      name: input.name,
      graph: JSON.stringify(input.graph),
      createdAt: new Date(),
      updatedAt: new Date(),
    });
    
    return { id };
  }
};

export const createWorkflowAction = async (input: {
  projectId: string;
  name: string;
}) => {
  const id = generateId();
  
  await db.insert(workflows).values({
    id,
    projectId: input.projectId,
    name: input.name,
    graph: JSON.stringify({ nodes: [], edges: [] }),
    createdAt: new Date(),
    updatedAt: new Date(),
  });
  
  return { id };
};
```

```typescript
// Using InferSelectModel for type-safe validation schemas
type TeamInvite = InferSelectModel<typeof teamInvites>;

export const teamInviteSchema = z.object({
  email: z.string().email(),
  roleId: z.string(),
  teamId: z.string(),
}) satisfies z.ZodType<Omit<TeamInvite, 'id' | 'token' | 'expiresAt' | 'createdAt'>>;

export const signUpSchema = z.object({
  email: z.string().email(),
  password: z.string().min(8),
  firstName: z.string().optional(),
  lastName: z.string().optional(),
  captchaToken: z.string(),
});
```

```typescript
interface SeparatorWithTextProps extends React.HTMLAttributes<HTMLDivElement> {
  children: React.ReactNode;
  leftBorderProps?: React.HTMLAttributes<HTMLDivElement>;
  rightBorderProps?: React.HTMLAttributes<HTMLDivElement>;
}

export function SeparatorWithText({ 
  children, 
  leftBorderProps, 
  rightBorderProps, 
  ...props 
}: SeparatorWithTextProps): React.JSX.Element {

  );
}
```

```typescript
// Declaration::passkeys::CALL, Declaration::passkeys.map::CALL, Declaration::passkeys.length::CALL
interface Passkey {
  credentialId: string;
  transports: string[];
}

export function usePasskeys() {
  const passkeys: Passkey[] = [];
  
  // Mapping pattern detected
  const mappedPasskeys = passkeys.map((passkey) => ({
    id: passkey.credentialId,
    transport: passkey.transports,
  }));
  
  // Length check pattern
  const hasPasskeys = passkeys.length > 0;
  
  return { passkeys, mappedPasskeys, hasPasskeys };
}

// Declaration::passkeyForm.control::CALL suggests React Hook Form integration
export function usePasskeyForm() {
  const passkeyForm = {
    control: {} as any, // Form control object
  };
  return passkeyForm;
}
```

```typescript
// Declaration::sqlStatements::CALL, Declaration::sqlStatements.push::CALL, Declaration::sqlStatements.length::CALL
export class SQLStatementBuilder {
  private sqlStatements: string[] = [];
  
  push(statement: string): void {
    this.sqlStatements.push(statement);
  }
  
  get length(): number {
    return this.sqlStatements.length;
  }
  
  build(): string[] {
    return this.sqlStatements;
  }
}
```

```typescript
// src/components/ui/spinner.tsx
interface SpinnerProps extends React.HTMLAttributes<HTMLDivElement> {
  size?: "sm" | "md" | "lg" | "xl";
  show?: boolean;
}

function Spinner({ className, size = "md", show = true, children, ...props }: SpinnerProps) {
  if (!show) return null;
  
  const sizeClasses = {
    sm: "h-4 w-4",
    md: "h-6 w-6",
    lg: "h-8 w-8",
    xl: "h-12 w-12"
  };

  return (
    <div
      className={cn("animate-spin", sizeClasses[size], className)}
      {...props}
    >
      {/* Spinner implementation */}
    </div>
  );
}

// src/components/ui/skeleton.tsx
function Skeleton({ className, ...props }: React.HTMLAttributes<HTMLDivElement>) {
  return (
    <div
      className={cn("animate-pulse rounded-md bg-muted", className)}
      {...props}
    />
  );
}
```

```typescript
import {

  addEdge,
  useReactFlow,
  Connection
} from '@xyflow/react'
import '@xyflow/react/dist/style.css'

interface FlowEditorContentProps {
  initialGraph?: any
  onSave?: (graph: any) => void
  onGenerate?: () => void
}

export function FlowEditorContent({ 
  initialGraph, 
  onSave, 
  onGenerate 
}: FlowEditorContentProps) {
  const [nodes, setNodes, onNodesChange] = useNodesState(initialGraph?.nodes || [])
  const [edges, setEdges, onEdgesChange] = useEdgesState(initialGraph?.edges || [])
  const reactFlowInstance = useReactFlow()

  const onConnect = useCallback((connection: Connection) => {
    setEdges((eds) => addEdge(connection, eds))
  }, [setEdges])

  // ... additional logic for node management
  // REFERENCES: useWorkflowStore, saveWorkflowAction, custom node types
}
```

```typescript
import { z } from "zod";

// Zod schema for React Flow node data
export const ArroNodeSchema = z.object({
  id: z.string(),
  type: z.string(),
  position: z.object({
    x: z.number(),
    y: z.number(),
  }),

  id: z.string(),

});

// Zod schema for complete workflow graph serialization

  nodes: z.array(ArroNodeSchema),
```

```typescript
  .input(WorkflowGraphSchema)
  .handler(async ({ input }) => {
    // VOCAB_MISSING: Implementation details
    // References: feNodes, beNodes, dbNodes conversion logic not visible
    const { nodes, edges } = input;
    // Serialization and DB update logic truncated
  });

// Server action to get workflow by ID
export const getWorkflowAction = createServerAction()
  .input(z.string())
  .handler(async ({ input }) => {
    const workflow = await getWorkflow(input);
    if (!workflow) throw new Error("Workflow not found");
    return workflow;
  });

// Server action to create new workflow
export const createWorkflowAction = createServerAction()
  .input(z.object({
    name: z.string(),
    projectId: z.string(),
  }))
  .handler(async ({ input }) => {
    // VOCAB_MISSING: Implementation not visible in atlas

    // DB insert logic truncated
  });

// Server action to get project workflows
export const getProjectWorkflowsAction = createServerAction()
  .input(z.string()) // projectId
  .handler(async ({ input }) => {
    return getProjectWorkflows(input);
  });
```

**File: `src/db/schema.ts`**
```typescript
import { pgTable, text, timestamp, integer, jsonb } from "drizzle-orm/pg-core";
import { relations } from "drizzle-orm";

export const workflowTable = pgTable("workflows", {
  id: text("id").primaryKey(),
  name: text("name").notNull(),
  projectId: text("project_id").notNull(),
  graphJson: text("graph_json").notNull(), // Serialized React Flow graph
  version: integer("version").notNull().default(1),
  updateCounter: integer("update_counter"),
  createdAt: timestamp("created_at").notNull().defaultNow(),
  updatedAt: timestamp("updated_at").notNull().defaultNow(),
});

// Relations configuration
export const workflowRelations = relations(workflowTable, ({ one }) => ({
  project: one(projectTable, {
    fields: [workflowTable.projectId],
    references: [projectTable.id],
  }),
}));

// VOCAB_MISSING: projectTable definition not visible in current atlas
declare const projectTable: any;
```

**File: `src/components/workflows/create-workflow-dialog.tsx`**
```typescript
"use client";

import { useState } from "react";
import { useServerAction } from "zsa-react";
import { createWorkflowAction } from "@/actions/workflow";
import {
  Dialog,
  DialogContent,
  DialogHeader,
  DialogTitle,
  DialogTrigger,
} from "@/components/ui/dialog";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
import { Input } from "@/components/ui/input";

interface CreateWorkflowDialogProps {
  trigger: React.ReactNode;
  projectId: string;
}

export function CreateWorkflowDialog({ trigger, projectId }: CreateWorkflowDialogProps) {
  const [name, setName] = useState("");
  const { execute, isPending } = useServerAction(createWorkflowAction, {
    onSuccess: () => {
      // Reset form or close dialog
    },
    onError: (error) => {
      // Error handling
    },
  });

  const handleSubmit = async (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    await execute({ name, projectId });
  };

  return (
    <Dialog>
      <DialogTrigger asChild>{trigger}</DialogTrigger>
      <DialogContent>
        <DialogHeader>
          <DialogTitle>Create Workflow</DialogTitle>
        </DialogHeader>
        <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="space-y-4">
          <Input
            value={name}
            onChange={(e) => setName(e.target.value)}
            placeholder="Workflow name"
          />
          <Button type="submit" disabled={isPending}>
            {isPending ? "Creating..." : "Create"}
          </Button>
        </form>
      </DialogContent>
    </Dialog>
  );
}
```

```typescript
import { Node, Edge } from "@xyflow/react";
import { NodeCategory } from "@/lib/arroflow/generator";

export interface NodeRule {

  condition?: string;
  targetNodeId?: string;
```

**File: `src/hooks/useWorkflow.ts`**
```typescript
import { useCallback, useState } from "react";
import { useReactFlow } from "@xyflow/react";
import { CustomNode, CustomEdge } from "@/types/workflow";

export function useWorkflow() {
  const { setNodes, setEdges, getNodes, getEdges } = useReactFlow();
  
  // Referenced patterns from metadata
  const updateNodes = useCallback((nextNodes: CustomNode[]) => {
    setNodes(nextNodes);
  }, [setNodes]);

  const updateEdges = useCallback((nextEdges: CustomEdge[]) => {
    setEdges(nextEdges);
  }, [setEdges]);

  const findNode = useCallback((nodeId: string) => {
    const nodes = getNodes();
    return nodes.find((node) => node.id === nodeId);
  }, [getNodes]);

  return {
    setNodes: updateNodes,
    setEdges: updateEdges,
    findNode
  };
}
```

**File: `src/app/actions/workflow.ts`**
```typescript
"use server";

import { db } from "@/db";
import { projectTable } from "@/db/schema";
import { eq } from "drizzle-orm";
import { revalidatePath } from "next/cache";

export async function saveWorkflowAction(
  projectId: string, 
  graphJson: string
) {
  await db
    .update(projectTable)
    .set({ 
      graphJson, 
      updatedAt: new Date() 
    })
    .where(eq(projectTable.id, projectId));
    
  revalidatePath(`/projects/${projectId}`);
}

export async function getWorkflowAction(projectId: string) {
  const project = await db.query.projectTable.findFirst({
    where: eq(projectTable.id, projectId),
    columns: { 
      graphJson: true,
      id: true,
      name: true
    }
  });
  
  return project;
}
```

**File: `src/components/canvas/node-context-menu.tsx` (Partial)**
```typescript
import {
  ContextMenu,
  ContextMenuTrigger,
  ContextMenuContent,
  ContextMenuItem,
  ContextMenuSub,
  ContextMenuSubTrigger,
  ContextMenuSubContent,
  ContextMenuCheckboxItem,
  ContextMenuRadioItem,
  ContextMenuRadioGroup,
  ContextMenuLabel,
  ContextMenuGroup,
  ContextMenuPortal,
  ContextMenuSeparator,
} from "@radix-ui/react-context-menu";
import { useReactFlow } from "@xyflow/react";

// Partial reconstruction based on metadata
export function NodeContextMenu({ children, nodeId }: { 
  children: React.ReactNode; 
  nodeId: string;
}) {
  const { getNode, setNodes, nodes } = useReactFlow();
  const selectedNode = getNode(nodeId);
  
  // Referenced in metadata: selectedNode.rules, selectedNode.properties, selectedNode.data.label
  const nodeRules = selectedNode?.data?.rules;
  const nodeProperties = selectedNode?.data?.properties;
  const nodeLabel = selectedNode?.data?.label;

  return (
    <ContextMenu>
      <ContextMenuTrigger>{children}</ContextMenuTrigger>
      <ContextMenuContent>
        <ContextMenuLabel>Node Actions</ContextMenuLabel>
        <ContextMenuSeparator />
        <ContextMenuGroup>
          <ContextMenuItem onSelect={() => {}}>
            Edit {nodeLabel}
          </ContextMenuItem>
        </ContextMenuGroup>
        {nodeRules && (
          <ContextMenuSub>
            <ContextMenuSubTrigger>Rules</ContextMenuSubTrigger>
            <ContextMenuSubContent>
              {nodeRules.map((rule) => (
                <ContextMenuCheckboxItem key={rule.id}>
                  {rule.condition}
                </ContextMenuCheckboxItem>
              ))}
            </ContextMenuSubContent>
          </ContextMenuSub>
        )}
        <ContextMenuPortal>
          <ContextMenuRadioGroup>
            <ContextMenuRadioItem value="option1">Option 1</ContextMenuRadioItem>
          </ContextMenuRadioGroup>
        </ContextMenuPortal>
      </ContextMenuContent>
    </ContextMenu>
  );
}
```

```typescript
import { pgTable, uuid, varchar, text, timestamp, json, integer, boolean } from "drizzle-orm/pg-core";
import { relations } from "drizzle-orm";

export const projectTable = pgTable("projects", {
  id: uuid("id").primaryKey().defaultRandom(),
  name: varchar("name", { length: 255 }).notNull(),
  description: text("description"),
  graphJson: json("graph_json"),
  ownerUserId: uuid("owner_user_id").notNull(),
  createdAt: timestamp("created_at").defaultNow().notNull(),
  updatedAt: timestamp("updated_at").defaultNow().notNull(),
});

export const userTable = pgTable("users", {
  id: uuid("id").primaryKey().defaultRandom(),
  email: varchar("email", { length: 255 }).notNull().unique(),
  firstName: varchar("first_name", { length: 255 }),
  lastName: varchar("last_name", { length: 255 }),
  currentCredits: integer("current_credits").default(0),
  emailVerified: boolean("email_verified").default(false),
  passwordHash: varchar("password_hash", { length: 255 }),
  lastCreditRefreshAt: timestamp("last_credit_refresh_at"),
  role: varchar("role", { length: 50 }),
  googleAccountId: varchar("google_account_id", { length: 255 }),
  avatar: varchar("avatar", { length: 500 }),
  createdAt: timestamp("created_at").defaultNow().notNull(),
  signUpIpAddress: varchar("sign_up_ip_address", { length: 45 }),
});

export const teamTable = pgTable("teams", {
  id: uuid("id").primaryKey().defaultRandom(),
  name: varchar("name", { length: 255 }).notNull(),
  slug: varchar("slug", { length: 255 }).notNull().unique(),
  description: text("description"),
  avatarUrl: varchar("avatar_url", { length: 500 }),
  creditBalance: integer("credit_balance").default(0),
});

export const teamMembershipTable = pgTable("team_memberships", {
  id: uuid("id").primaryKey().defaultRandom(),
  teamId: uuid("team_id").notNull().references(() => teamTable.id),
  userId: uuid("user_id").notNull().references(() => userTable.id),
  roleId: uuid("role_id").notNull(),
  isSystemRole: boolean("is_system_role").default(false),
  invitedBy: uuid("invited_by").references(() => userTable.id),
  invitedAt: timestamp("invited_at"),
  joinedAt: timestamp("joined_at"),
  isActive: boolean("is_active").default(true),
});

export const teamInvitationTable = pgTable("team_invitations", {
  id: uuid("id").primaryKey().defaultRandom(),
  teamId: uuid("team_id").notNull().references(() => teamTable.id),
  email: varchar("email", { length: 255 }).notNull(),
  roleId: uuid("role_id").notNull(),
  isSystemRole: boolean("is_system_role").default(false),
  token: varchar("token", { length: 255 }).notNull().unique(),
  invitedBy: uuid("invited_by").notNull().references(() => userTable.id),
  expiresAt: timestamp("expires_at").notNull(),
  acceptedAt: timestamp("accepted_at"),
  acceptedBy: uuid("accepted_by").references(() => userTable.id),
  updatedAt: timestamp("updated_at").defaultNow().notNull(),
});

export const creditTransactionTable = pgTable("credit_transactions", {
  id: uuid("id").primaryKey().defaultRandom(),
  userId: uuid("user_id").notNull().references(() => userTable.id),
  amount: integer("amount").notNull(),
  remainingAmount: integer("remaining_amount").notNull(),
  type: varchar("type", { length: 50 }).notNull(),
  description: text("description"),
  expirationDate: timestamp("expiration_date"),
  paymentIntentId: varchar("payment_intent_id", { length: 255 }),
  createdAt: timestamp("created_at").defaultNow().notNull(),
  updatedAt: timestamp("updated_at").defaultNow().notNull(),
});

export const passKeyCredentialTable = pgTable("passkey_credentials", {
  id: uuid("id").primaryKey().defaultRandom(),
  userId: uuid("user_id").notNull().references(() => userTable.id),
  credentialId: varchar("credential_id", { length: 255 }).notNull(),
  credentialPublicKey: text("credential_public_key").notNull(),
  counter: integer("counter").default(0),
  transports: json("transports"),
  aaguid: varchar("aaguid", { length: 255 }),
  userAgent: text("user_agent"),
  ipAddress: varchar("ip_address", { length: 45 }),
});
```

**File: `src/app/actions/workflow.ts` (Server Actions)**

```typescript
"use server";

import { z } from "zod";
import { SaveWorkflowSchema, GetWorkflowSchema } from "@/schemas/workflow";
import { and, eq } from "drizzle-orm";
import { db } from "@/db"; // VOCAB_MISSING: exact db import
import { workflows } from "@/db/schema"; // VOCAB_MISSING: exact schema

// Save Workflow Action - reconstructed from metadata variations
export const saveWorkflowAction = async (input: unknown) => {
  const validated = SaveWorkflowSchema.parse(input);
  const { workflowId, graphJson } = validated;
  
  // Database operation inferred from drizzle-orm usage
  await db.update(workflows)
    .set({ graphJson, updatedAt: new Date() })
    .where(and(
      eq(workflows.id, workflowId),
      // Additional conditions not visible
    ));
    
  return { success: true };
};

// Get Workflow Action
export const getWorkflowAction = async (input: unknown) => {
  const validated = GetWorkflowSchema.parse(input);
  const { workflowId } = validated;
  
  const workflow = await db.query.workflows.findFirst({
    where: eq(workflows.id, workflowId)
  });
  
  if (!workflow) {
    throw new Error("Workflow not found");
  }
  
  return {
    nodes: workflow.nodes,
    edges: workflow.edges,
    project: workflow.project
  };
};
```

```typescript
// src/app/api/get-session/route.ts
import { NextResponse } from "next/server";
import { validateSession } from "@/lib/session";

export async function GET() {
  const session = await validateSession();
  return NextResponse.json({
    session,
    config: {
      isGoogleSSOEnabled: process.env.GOOGLE_SSO_ENABLED === "true",
      isTurnstileEnabled: process.env.TURNSTILE_ENABLED === "true",
    },
  });
}
```

```typescript
// src/app/settings/settings/sessions/sessions_client.tsx
"use client";

import { useState } from "react";
import { Card, CardContent, CardHeader, CardTitle } from "@/components/ui/card";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
import { Badge } from "@/components/ui/badge";
import { toast } from "sonner";
import { revokeSession } from "@/app/actions/session";

interface SessionWithMeta {
  id: string;
  userId: string;
  expiresAt: Date;
  country?: string;
  city?: string;
  isCurrentSession: boolean;
  authenticationType: "password" | "passkey" | "oauth";
  createdAt: Date;
  user: {
    email: string;
    firstName?: string;
    lastName?: string;
  };
}

interface SessionsClientProps {
  sessions: SessionWithMeta[];
}

export function SessionsClient({ sessions }: SessionsClientProps) {
  const [existingSessions, setExistingSessions] = useState(sessions);
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState<string | null>(null);

  const handleRevoke = async (sessionId: string) => {
    setIsLoading(sessionId);
    try {
      await revokeSession(sessionId);
      setExistingSessions((prev) => 
        prev.filter((s) => s.id !== sessionId)
      );
      toast.success("Session revoked successfully");
    } catch (error) {
      toast.error("Failed to revoke session");
    } finally {
      setIsLoading(null);
    }
  };

  if (existingSessions.length === 0) {
    return (
      <Card>
        <CardHeader>
          <CardTitle>Active Sessions</CardTitle>
        </CardHeader>
        <CardContent>
          <p className="text-muted-foreground">No active sessions found.</p>
        </CardContent>
      </Card>
    );
  }

  return (
    <div className="space-y-4">
      {existingSessions.map((session) => (
        <Card key={session.id} className={session.isCurrentSession ? "border-primary" : ""}>
          <CardContent className="flex items-center justify-between p-4">
            <div className="space-y-1">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                <span className="font-medium">
                  {session.city}, {session.country}
                </span>
                {session.isCurrentSession && (
                  <Badge variant="default">Current</Badge>
                )}
                <Badge variant="outline">{session.authenticationType}</Badge>
              </div>
              <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
                Created: {new Date(session.createdAt).toLocaleString()}
              </p>
              <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
                Expires: {new Date(session.expiresAt).toLocaleString()}
              </p>
            </div>
            {!session.isCurrentSession && (
              <Button
                variant="destructive"
                size="sm"
                onClick={() => handleRevoke(session.id)}
                disabled={isLoading === session.id}
              >
                Revoke
              </Button>
            )}
          </CardContent>
        </Card>
      ))}
    </div>
  );
}
```

```typescript
// src/app/settings/settings/security/passkey_client.tsx
"use client";

import { useState } from "react";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
import { Card, CardContent, CardDescription, CardHeader, CardTitle } from "@/components/ui/card";
import { toast } from "sonner";
import { startRegistration } from "@simplewebauthn/browser";

interface PasskeyRegistrationButtonProps {
  email: string;
  className?: string;
  onSuccess?: () => void;
}

export function PasskeyRegistrationButton({ 
  email, 
  className, 
  onSuccess 
}: PasskeyRegistrationButtonProps) {
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);

  const handleRegister = async () => {
    setIsLoading(true);
    try {
      // Get challenge from server
      const challengeRes = await fetch("/api/auth/passkey/challenge", {
        method: "POST",
        headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        body: JSON.stringify({ email }),
      });
      
      const challenge = await challengeRes.json();
      
      // Start WebAuthn registration
      const attestation = await startRegistration(challenge);
      
      // Verify with server
      const verifyRes = await fetch("/api/auth/passkey/verify", {
        method: "POST",
        headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        body: JSON.stringify({
          email,
          attestation,
        }),
      });

      if (verifyRes.ok) {
        toast.success("Passkey registered successfully");
        onSuccess?.();
      } else {
        throw new Error("Verification failed");
      }
    } catch (error) {
      toast.error("Failed to register passkey");
      console.error(error);
    } finally {
      setIsLoading(false);
    }
  };

  return (
    <Button 
      onClick={handleRegister} 
      disabled={isLoading}
      className={className}
    >
      {isLoading ? "Registering..." : "Register Passkey"}
    </Button>
  );
}

interface Passkey {
  id: string;
  credentialId: string;
  createdAt: Date;
  lastUsedAt?: Date;
}

interface PasskeysListProps {
  passkeys: Passkey[];
  currentPasskeyId?: string;
  email: string;
}

export function PasskeysList({ passkeys, currentPasskeyId, email }: PasskeysListProps) {
  const [isDeleting, setIsDeleting] = useState<string | null>(null);

  const handleDelete = async (passkeyId: string) => {
    setIsDeleting(passkeyId);
    try {
      await fetch("/api/auth/passkey/delete", {
        method: "POST",
        headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        body: JSON.stringify({ passkeyId, email }),
      });
      toast.success("Passkey removed");
    } catch (error) {
      toast.error("Failed to remove passkey");
    } finally {
      setIsDeleting(null);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="space-y-4">
      {passkeys.map((passkey) => (
        <Card key={passkey.id}>
          <CardContent className="flex items-center justify-between p-4">
            <div>
              <p className="font-medium">
                Passkey {passkey.credentialId.slice(0, 8)}...
                {passkey.id === currentPasskeyId && " (Current)"}
              </p>
              <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
                Created: {new Date(passkey.createdAt).toLocaleDateString()}
              </p>
            </div>
            <Button
              variant="destructive"
              size="sm"
              onClick={() => handleDelete(passkey.id)}
              disabled={isDeleting === passkey.id}
            >
              Remove
            </Button>
          </CardContent>
        </Card>
      ))}
    </div>
  );
}
```

```typescript
// src/app/auth/components/sso-buttons.tsx
"use client";

import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
import { Chrome } from "lucide-react";

interface SSOButtonsProps {
  isSignIn?: boolean;
}

export function SSOButtons({ isSignIn = true }: SSOButtonsProps) {
  const handleGoogleSignIn = () => {
    const redirectUri = encodeURIComponent(
      `${window.location.origin}/auth/sso/google/callback`
    );
    const googleAuthUrl = `https://accounts.google.com/o/oauth2/v2/auth?client_id=${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID}&redirect_uri=${redirectUri}&response_type=code&scope=email profile`;
    
    window.location.href = googleAuthUrl;
  };

  return (
    <div className="grid gap-2">
      <Button
        variant="outline"
        onClick={handleGoogleSignIn}
        className="w-full"
      >
        <Chrome className="mr-2 h-4 w-4" />
        {isSignIn ? "Sign in with Google" : "Sign up with Google"}
      </Button>
    </div>
  );
}
```

```typescript
// src/app/auth/sso/google/route.ts
import { NextResponse } from "next/server";

export async function GET() {
  const redirectUri = `${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_APP_URL}/auth/sso/google/callback`;
  const googleAuthUrl = new URL("https://accounts.google.com/o/oauth2/v2/auth");
  
  googleAuthUrl.searchParams.set("client_id", process.env.GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID!);
  googleAuthUrl.searchParams.set("redirect_uri", redirectUri);
  googleAuthUrl.searchParams.set("response_type", "code");
  googleAuthUrl.searchParams.set("scope", "email profile");
  googleAuthUrl.searchParams.set("access_type", "offline");
  googleAuthUrl.searchParams.set("prompt", "consent");

  return NextResponse.redirect(googleAuthUrl.toString());
}
```

```typescript
// src/app/auth/sso/google/callback/page.tsx
import { redirect } from "next/navigation";
import { GoogleCallbackClientComponent } from "./google-callback_client";

export default function GoogleCallbackPage({
  searchParams,
}: {
  searchParams: { code?: string; error?: string };
}) {
  if (searchParams.error) {
    redirect("/auth/sign-in?error=oauth_failed");
  }

  if (!searchParams.code) {
    redirect("/auth/sign-in?error=no_code");
  }

  return <GoogleCallbackClientComponent code={searchParams.code} />;
}
```

```typescript
// src/app/auth/sso/google/callback/google-callback_client.tsx
"use client";

import { useEffect, useState } from "react";
import { useRouter } from "next/navigation";
import { toast } from "sonner";

interface GoogleCallbackClientComponentProps {
  code: string;
}

export function GoogleCallbackClientComponent({ 
  code 
}: GoogleCallbackClientComponentProps) {
  const router = useRouter();
  const [isProcessing, setIsProcessing] = useState(true);

  useEffect(() => {
    async function handleCallback() {
      try {
        const response = await fetch("/api/auth/sso/google/callback", {
          method: "POST",
          headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
          body: JSON.stringify({ code }),
        });

        if (!response.ok) {
          throw new Error("Authentication failed");
        }

        const data = await response.json();
        
        // Session cookie is set by server
        toast.success("Signed in successfully");
        router.push(data.redirectTo || "/dashboard");
      } catch (error) {
        toast.error("Failed to sign in with Google");
        router.push("/auth/sign-in?error=oauth_failed");
      } finally {
        setIsProcessing(false);
      }
    }

    handleCallback();
  }, [code, router]);

  if (isProcessing) {
    return (
      <div className="flex items-center justify-center min-h-screen">
        <div className="animate-spin rounded-full h-8 w-8 border-b-2 border-primary" />
      </div>
    );
  }

  return null;
}
```

```typescript
// src/app/auth/sign-in/sign-in_client.tsx
"use client";

import { useState } from "react";
import { useRouter } from "next/navigation";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
import { Input } from "@/components/ui/input";
import { Label } from "@/components/ui/label";
import { toast } from "sonner";
import { startAuthentication } from "@simplewebauthn/browser";

interface SignInPageProps {
  redirectPath?: string;
}

export function SignInPage({ redirectPath = "/dashboard" }: SignInPageProps) {
  const [email, setEmail] = useState("");
  const [password, setPassword] = useState("");
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);
  const router = useRouter();

  const handleSubmit = async (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    setIsLoading(true);

    try {
      const response = await fetch("/api/auth/sign-in", {
        method: "POST",
        headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        body: JSON.stringify({ email, password }),
      });

      if (!response.ok) {
        throw new Error("Invalid credentials");
      }

      toast.success("Signed in successfully");
      router.push(redirectPath);
      router.refresh();
    } catch (error) {
      toast.error("Failed to sign in");
    } finally {
      setIsLoading(false);
    }
  };

  return (
    <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="space-y-4">
      <div className="space-y-2">
        <Label htmlFor="email">Email</Label>
        <Input
          id="email"
          type="email"
          value={email}
          onChange={(e) => setEmail(e.target.value)}
          required
        />
      </div>
      <div className="space-y-2">
        <Label htmlFor="password">Password</Label>
        <Input
          id="password"
          type="password"
          value={password}
          onChange={(e) => setPassword(e.target.value)}
          required
        />
      </div>
      <Button type="submit" className="w-full" disabled={isLoading}>
        {isLoading ? "Signing in..." : "Sign In"}
      </Button>
    </form>
  );
}

interface PasskeyAuthenticationButtonProps {
  className?: string;
  disabled?: boolean;
  children?: React.ReactNode;
  redirectPath?: string;
}

export function PasskeyAuthenticationButton({
  className,
  disabled,
  children,
  redirectPath = "/dashboard",
}: PasskeyAuthenticationButtonProps) {
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);
  const router = useRouter();

  const handlePasskeySignIn = async () => {
    setIsLoading(true);
    try {
      // Get authentication options
      const optionsRes = await fetch("/api/auth/passkey/authenticate", {
        method: "POST",
      });
      const options = await optionsRes.json();

      // Start WebAuthn authentication
      const assertion = await startAuthentication(options);

      // Verify assertion
      const verifyRes = await fetch("/api/auth/passkey/authenticate/verify", {
        method: "POST",
        headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        body: JSON.stringify(assertion),
      });

      if (verifyRes.ok) {
        toast.success("Signed in with passkey");
        router.push(redirectPath);
        router.refresh();
      } else {
        throw new Error("Authentication failed");
      }
    } catch (error) {
      toast.error("Passkey authentication failed");
    } finally {
      setIsLoading(false);
    }
  };

  return (
    <Button
      variant="outline"
      onClick={handlePasskeySignIn}
      disabled={disabled || isLoading}
      className={className}
    >
      {children || "Sign in with Passkey"}
    </Button>
  );
}
```

```typescript
// src/components/ui/badge.tsx
import * as React from "react"
import { cva, type VariantProps } from "class-variance-authority"
import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"

const badgeVariants = cva(
  "inline-flex items-center rounded-full border px-2.5 py-0.5 text-xs font-semibold transition-colors focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-ring focus:ring-offset-2",
  {
    variants: {
      variant: {
        default:
          "border-transparent bg-primary text-primary-foreground hover:bg-primary/80",
        secondary:
          "border-transparent bg-secondary text-secondary-foreground hover:bg-secondary/80",
        destructive:
          "border-transparent bg-destructive text-destructive-foreground hover:bg-destructive/80",
        outline: "text-foreground",
      },
    },
    defaultVariants: {
      variant: "default",
    },
  }
)

export interface BadgeProps
  extends React.HTMLAttributes<HTMLDivElement>,
    VariantProps<typeof badgeVariants> {}

function Badge({ className, variant, ...props }: BadgeProps) {
  return (
    <div className={cn(badgeVariants({ variant }), className)} {...props} />
  )
}

export { Badge, badgeVariants }
```

```typescript
// src/components/ui/sheet.tsx
import * as React from "react"
import * as SheetPrimitive from "@radix-ui/react-dialog"
import { cva, type VariantProps } from "class-variance-authority"
import { X } from "lucide-react"
import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"

const Sheet = SheetPrimitive.Root

const SheetTrigger = SheetPrimitive.Trigger

const SheetClose = SheetPrimitive.Close

const SheetPortal = SheetPrimitive.Portal

const SheetOverlay = React.forwardRef<
  React.ElementRef<typeof SheetPrimitive.Overlay>,
  React.ComponentPropsWithoutRef<typeof SheetPrimitive.Overlay>
>(({ className, ...props }, ref) => (
  <SheetPrimitive.Overlay
    className={cn(
      "fixed inset-0 z-50 bg-black/80 data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:fade-out-0 data-[state=open]:fade-in-0",
      className
    )}
    {...props}
    ref={ref}
  />
))
SheetOverlay.displayName = SheetPrimitive.Overlay.displayName

const sheetVariants = cva(
  "fixed z-50 gap-4 bg-background p-6 shadow-lg transition ease-in-out data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:duration-300 data-[state=open]:duration-500",
  {
    variants: {
      side: {
        top: "inset-x-0 top-0 border-b data-[state=closed]:slide-out-to-top data-[state=open]:slide-in-from-top",
        bottom:
          "inset-x-0 bottom-0 border-t data-[state=closed]:slide-out-to-bottom data-[state=open]:slide-in-from-bottom",
        left: "inset-y-0 left-0 h-full w-3/4 border-r data-[state=closed]:slide-out-to-left data-[state=open]:slide-in-from-left sm:max-w-sm",
        right:
          "inset-y-0 right-0 h-full w-3/4 border-l data-[state=closed]:slide-out-to-right data-[state=open]:slide-in-from-right sm:max-w-sm",
      },
    },
    defaultVariants: {
      side: "right",
    },
  }
)

interface SheetContentProps
  extends React.ComponentPropsWithoutRef<typeof SheetPrimitive.Content>,
    VariantProps<typeof sheetVariants> {}

const SheetContent = React.forwardRef<
  React.ElementRef<typeof SheetPrimitive.Content>,
  SheetContentProps
>(({ side = "right", className, children, ...props }, ref) => (
  <SheetPortal>
    <SheetOverlay />
    <SheetPrimitive.Content
      ref={ref}
      className={cn(sheetVariants({ side }), className)}
      {...props}
    >
      {children}
      <SheetPrimitive.Close className="absolute right-4 top-4 rounded-sm opacity-70 ring-offset-background transition-opacity hover:opacity-100 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-ring focus:ring-offset-2 disabled:pointer-events-none data-[state=open]:bg-secondary">
        <X className="h-4 w-4" />
        <span className="sr-only">Close</span>
      </SheetPrimitive.Close>
    </SheetPrimitive.Content>
  </SheetPortal>
))
SheetContent.displayName = SheetPrimitive.Content.displayName

const SheetHeader = ({
  className,
  ...props
}: React.HTMLAttributes<HTMLDivElement>) => (
  <div
    className={cn(
      "flex flex-col space-y-2 text-center sm:text-left",
      className
    )}
    {...props}
  />
)
SheetHeader.displayName = "SheetHeader"

const SheetFooter = ({
  className,
  ...props
}: React.HTMLAttributes<HTMLDivElement>) => (
  <div
    className={cn(
      "flex flex-col-reverse sm:flex-row sm:justify-end sm:space-x-2",
      className
    )}
    {...props}
  />
)
SheetFooter.displayName = "SheetFooter"

const SheetTitle = React.forwardRef<
  React.ElementRef<typeof SheetPrimitive.Title>,
  React.ComponentPropsWithoutRef<typeof SheetPrimitive.Title>
>(({ className, ...props }, ref) => (
  <SheetPrimitive.Title
    ref={ref}
    className={cn("text-lg font-semibold text-foreground", className)}
    {...props}
  />
))
SheetTitle.displayName = SheetPrimitive.Title.displayName

const SheetDescription = React.forwardRef<
  React.ElementRef<typeof SheetPrimitive.Description>,
  React.ComponentPropsWithoutRef<typeof SheetPrimitive.Description>
>(({ className, ...props }, ref) => (
  <SheetPrimitive.Description
    ref={ref}
    className={cn("text-sm text-muted-foreground", className)}
    {...props}
  />
))
SheetDescription.displayName = SheetPrimitive.Description.displayName

export {
  Sheet,
  SheetPortal,
  SheetOverlay,
  SheetTrigger,
  SheetClose,
  SheetContent,
  SheetHeader,
  SheetFooter,
  SheetTitle,
  SheetDescription,
```

```typescript
// src/components/ui/spinner.tsx
import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"

interface SpinnerProps {
  size?: "sm" | "md" | "lg"
  show?: boolean
  children?: React.ReactNode
  className?: string
}

function Spinner({ size = "md", show = true, children, className }: SpinnerProps) {
  if (!show) return null
  
  const sizeClasses = {
    sm: "h-4 w-4",
    md: "h-6 w-6",
    lg: "h-8 w-8"
  }

  return (
    <div className={cn("flex items-center justify-center", className)}>
      <div
        className={cn(
          "animate-spin rounded-full border-2 border-current border-t-transparent",
          sizeClasses[size]
        )}
      />
      {children}
    </div>
  )
}

export { Spinner }
```
