Based on the code atlas and metadata analysis, I have reconstructed the authentication and session management system architecture. The atlas reveals a comprehensive auth system using ZSA server actions, KV storage for sessions, WebAuthn for passkeys, and Drizzle ORM for database operations.

### A) RECONSTRUCTED CODE

**src/utils/auth.ts**
```typescript
import { cookies } from "next/headers";
import { db } from "@/db";
import { userTable, passKeyCredentialTable, teamMembershipTable, teamTable, teamInvitationTable } from "@/db/schema";
import { eq, and, sql } from "drizzle-orm";
import { getKV } from "@/utils/kv";
import { hashPassword } from "@/utils/password-hasher";
import { generatePasskeyRegistrationOptions, verifyPasskeyRegistration } from "@/utils/webauthn";
import { sendVerificationEmail, sendTeamInvitationEmail } from "@/utils/email";
import { getIP } from "@/utils/get-IP";
import { generateSlug } from "@/utils/slugify";
import { getVerificationTokenKey, getResetTokenKey } from "@/utils/auth-utils";

// Session types inferred from metadata
interface KVSession {
  userId: string;
  authenticationType: "password" | "passkey" | "google";
  passkeyCredentialId?: string;
  absoluteExpiration: Date;
  teams: Array<{
    id: string;
    name: string;
    slug: string;
    role: {
      id: string;
      name: string;
      isSystemRole: boolean;
    };
    permissions: string[];
  }>;
}

interface SetSessionTokenCookieParams {
  token: string;
  expires: Date;
  isSecure?: boolean;
}

interface CreateKVSessionParams {
  authenticationType: "password" | "passkey" | "google";
  passkeyCredentialId?: string;
}

// Generate cryptographically secure session token
export function generateSessionToken(): string {
  // Implementation uses crypto.randomBytes or Web Crypto API
  const token = Array.from(crypto.getRandomValues(new Uint8Array(32)))
    .map(b => b.toString(16).padStart(2, '0'))
    .join('');
  return token;
}

// Create session in KV storage and set cookie
export async function createAndStoreSession(
  userId: string,
  authenticationType: CreateKVSessionParams["authenticationType"],
  passkeyCredentialId?: CreateKVSessionParams["passkeyCredentialId"]
): Promise<void> {
  const token = generateSessionToken();
  const sessionId = generateSessionId(token);
  
  // Calculate expiration (e.g., 30 days)
  const absoluteExpiration = new Date(Date.now() + 30 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
  
  // Get user teams for session context
  const teams = await getUserTeamsWithPermissions(userId);
  
  const sessionObj: KVSession = {
    userId,
    authenticationType,
    passkeyCredentialId,
    absoluteExpiration,
    teams
  };
  
  // Store in KV with expiration
  const kv = getKV();
  await kv.put(`session:${sessionId}`, JSON.stringify(sessionObj), {
    expirationTtl: Math.floor((absoluteExpiration.getTime() - Date.now()) / 1000)
  });
  
  // Set HTTP-only cookie
  await setSessionTokenCookie({
    token,
    expires: absoluteExpiration,
    isSecure: process.env.NODE_ENV === "production"
  });
}

// Set session cookie with security flags
export async function setSessionTokenCookie(params: SetSessionTokenCookieParams): Promise<void> {
  const { token, expires, isSecure = true } = params;
  const cookieStore = await cookies();
  
  cookieStore.set("session-token", token, {
    httpOnly: true,
    secure: isSecure,
    sameSite: "lax",
    expires,
    path: "/"
  });
}

// Validate session from cookie and KV
export async function getSessionFromCookie(): Promise<{ session: KVSession | null; user: typeof userTable.$inferSelect | null }> {
  const cookieStore = await cookies();
  const token = cookieStore.get("session-token")?.value;
  
  if (!token) {
    return { session: null, user: null };
  }
  
  const sessionId = generateSessionId(token);
  const kv = getKV();
  const sessionData = await kv.get(`session:${sessionId}`);
  
  if (!sessionData) {
    return { session: null, user: null };
  }
  
  const session: KVSession = JSON.parse(sessionData);
  
  // Check expiration
  if (new Date() > new Date(session.absoluteExpiration)) {
    await kv.delete(`session:${sessionId}`);
    return { session: null, user: null };
  }
  
  // Fetch fresh user data
  const user = await getUserFromDB(session.userId);
  
  if (!user) {
    return { session: null, user: null };
  }
  
  return { session, user };
}

// Clear session on logout
export async function clearSession(): Promise<void> {
  const cookieStore = await cookies();
  const token = cookieStore.get("session-token")?.value;
  
  if (token) {
    const sessionId = generateSessionId(token);
    const kv = getKV();
    await kv.delete(`session:${sessionId}`);
  }
  
  cookieStore.delete("session-token");
}

// Get user from database with selected fields
export async function getUserFromDB(userId: string): Promise<{
  id: string;
  firstName: string | null;
  lastName: string | null;
  email: string | null;
  role: string;
  emailVerified: Date | null;
  avatar: string | null;
  currentCredits: number;
  lastCreditRefreshAt: Date | null;
  createdAt: Date;
  updatedAt: Date;
} | undefined> {
  const user = await db.query.userTable.findFirst({
    where: eq(userTable.id, userId),
    columns: {
      id: true,
      firstName: true,
      lastName: true,
      email: true,
      role: true,
      emailVerified: true,
      avatar: true,
      currentCredits: true,
      lastCreditRefreshAt: true,
      createdAt: true,
      updatedAt: true
    }
  });
  
  return user;
}

// Get user teams with role permissions
export async function getUserTeamsWithPermissions(userId: string): Promise<Array<{
  id: string;
  name: string;
  slug: string;
  role: {
    id: string;
    name: string;
    isSystemRole: boolean;
  };
  permissions: string[];
}>> {
  const memberships = await db.query.teamMembershipTable.findMany({
    where: eq(teamMembershipTable.userId, userId),
    with: {
      team: true,
      role: true
    }
  });
  
  return memberships.map(m => ({
    id: m.team.id,
    name: m.team.name,
    slug: m.team.slug,
    role: {
      id: m.role.id,
      name: m.role.name,
      isSystemRole: m.role.isSystemRole
    },
    permissions: m.role.permissions || []
  }));
}

// Check if user has specific team permission
export async function hasTeamPermission(userId: string, permission: string): Promise<boolean> {
  const teams = await getUserTeamsWithPermissions(userId);
  return teams.some(t => t.permissions.includes(permission));
}

// Require verified email middleware
export async function requireVerifiedEmail(params?: { doNotThrowError?: boolean }): Promise<KVSession> {
  const { session, user } = await getSessionFromCookie();
  
  if (!session || !user) {
    if (params?.doNotThrowError) return null as any;
    throw new Error("Unauthorized");
  }
  
  if (!user.emailVerified) {
    if (params?.doNotThrowError) return null as any;
    throw new Error("Email not verified");
  }
  
  return session;
}

// Require admin role
export async function requireAdmin(params?: { doNotThrowError?: boolean }): Promise<KVSession | null> {
  const { session, user } = await getSessionFromCookie();
  
  if (!session || !user || user.role !== "admin") {
    if (params?.doNotThrowError) return null;
    throw new Error("Forbidden");
  }
  
  return session;
}

// Validate signup eligibility (disposable email check)
export async function canSignUp(params: { 
  email: string; 
  skipDisposableEmailCheck?: boolean 
}): Promise<void> {
  const { email, skipDisposableEmailCheck } = params;
  
  if (!skipDisposableEmailCheck) {
    // Check against disposable email list via KV or API
    const kv = getKV();
    const isDisposable = await kv.get(`disposable-email:${email.split('@')[1]}`);
    if (isDisposable) {
      throw new Error("Disposable email addresses are not allowed");
    }
  }
  
  // Check if email already exists
  const existing = await db.query.userTable.findFirst({
    where: eq(userTable.email, email),
    columns: { id: true }
  });
  
  if (existing) {
    throw new Error("Email already registered");
  }
}

// Generate session ID from token (hashing for KV key)
function generateSessionId(token: string): string {
  // Implementation uses SHA-256 or similar
  return crypto.subtle.digest('SHA-256', new TextEncoder().encode(token))
    .then(buf => Array.from(new Uint8Array(buf)).map(b => b.toString(16).padStart(2, '0')).join(''));
}
```

**src/utils/webauthn.ts**
```typescript
import { generateRegistrationOptions, verifyRegistrationResponse, generateAuthenticationOptions, verifyAuthenticationResponse } from "@simplewebauthn/server";
import { db } from "@/db";
import { passKeyCredentialTable } from "@/db/schema";
import { eq } from "drizzle-orm";

// Generate registration options for new passkey
export async function generatePasskeyRegistrationOptions(
  userId: string,
  username: string
): Promise<PublicKeyCredentialCreationOptionsJSON> {
  const options = await generateRegistrationOptions({
    rpName: process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_APP_NAME || "App",
    rpID: process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_RP_ID || "localhost",
    userID: userId,
    userName: username,
    userDisplayName: username,
    attestationType: "none",
    authenticatorSelection: {
      residentKey: "preferred",
      userVerification: "preferred",
      authenticatorAttachment: "platform"
    }
  });
  
  // Store challenge in KV for verification
  const kv = getKV();
  await kv.put(`challenge:${userId}`, options.challenge, {
    expirationTtl: 300 // 5 minutes
  });
  
  return options;
}

// Verify passkey registration response
export async function verifyPasskeyRegistration(params: {
  userId: string;
  response: RegistrationResponseJSON;
  challenge: string;
  userAgent?: string | null;
  ipAddress?: string | null;
}): Promise<{
  credential: typeof passKeyCredentialTable.$inferSelect;
  success: boolean;
}> {
  const { userId, response, challenge, userAgent, ipAddress } = params;
  
  const verification = await verifyRegistrationResponse({
    response,
    expectedChallenge: challenge,
    expectedOrigin: process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_APP_URL || "http://localhost:3000",
    expectedRPID: process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_RP_ID || "localhost"
  });
  
  if (!verification.verified || !verification.registrationInfo) {
    throw new Error("Passkey verification failed");
  }
  
  const { credential } = verification.registrationInfo;
  
  // Store credential in database
  const [passkey] = await db.insert(passKeyCredentialTable).values({
    userId,
    credentialId: credential.id,
    credentialPublicKey: Buffer.from(credential.publicKey).toString("base64"),
    counter: credential.counter,
    transports: response.response.transports || [],
    aaguid: credential.aaguid || null,
    userAgent: userAgent || null,
    ipAddress: ipAddress || null
  }).returning();
  
  return { credential: passkey, success: true };
}
```

**src/db/schema.ts** (Auth-related tables)
```typescript
import { pgTable, uuid, varchar, timestamp, integer, boolean, text, jsonb, real } from "drizzle-orm/pg-core";
import { relations } from "drizzle-orm";

// Users table
export const userTable = pgTable("users", {
  id: uuid("id").primaryKey().defaultRandom(),
  email: varchar("email", { length: 255 }).unique().notNull(),
  firstName: varchar("first_name", { length: 100 }),
  lastName: varchar("last_name", { length: 100 }),
  passwordHash: varchar("password_hash", { length: 255 }),
  emailVerified: timestamp("email_verified", { withTimezone: true }),
  googleAccountId: varchar("google_account_id", { length: 255 }).unique(),
  avatar: varchar("avatar", { length: 500 }),
  role: varchar("role", { length: 50 }).default("user").notNull(),
  currentCredits: real("current_credits").default(0).notNull(),
  lastCreditRefreshAt: timestamp("last_credit_refresh_at", { withTimezone: true }),
  signUpIpAddress: varchar("sign_up_ip_address", { length: 45 }),
  createdAt: timestamp("created_at", { withTimezone: true }).defaultNow().notNull(),
  updatedAt: timestamp("updated_at", { withTimezone: true }).defaultNow().notNull()
});

// Passkey credentials table
export const passKeyCredentialTable = pgTable("passkey_credentials", {
  id: uuid("id").primaryKey().defaultRandom(),
  userId: uuid("user_id").references(() => userTable.id, { onDelete: "cascade" }).notNull(),
  credentialId: varchar("credential_id", { length: 255 }).notNull().unique(),
  credentialPublicKey: text("credential_public_key").notNull(),
  counter: integer("counter").default(0).notNull(),
  transports: jsonb("transports").$type<string[]>().default([]),
  aaguid: varchar("aaguid", { length: 36 }),
  userAgent: text("user_agent"),
  ipAddress: varchar("ip_address", { length: 45 }),
  createdAt: timestamp("created_at", { withTimezone: true }).defaultNow().notNull(),
  updatedAt: timestamp("updated_at", { withTimezone: true }).defaultNow().notNull()
});

// Credit transactions (for billing/credits system)
export const creditTransactionTable = pgTable("credit_transactions", {
  id: uuid("id").primaryKey().defaultRandom(),
  userId: uuid("user_id").references(() => userTable.id, { onDelete: "cascade" }).notNull(),
  amount: real("amount").notNull(),
  remainingAmount: real("remaining_amount").notNull(),
  type: varchar("type", { length: 50 }).notNull(), // 'purchase', 'usage', 'refund'
  description: text("description"),
  paymentIntentId: varchar("payment_intent_id", { length: 255 }),
  expirationDate: timestamp("expiration_date", { withTimezone: true }),
  expirationDateProcessedAt: timestamp("expiration_date_processed_at", { withTimezone: true }),
  createdAt: timestamp("created_at", { withTimezone: true }).defaultNow().notNull()
});

// Relations
export const userRelations = relations(userTable, ({ many }) => ({
  passkeys: many(passKeyCredentialTable),
  creditTransactions: many(creditTransactionTable),
  teamMemberships: many(teamMembershipTable)
}));

export const creditTransactionRelations = relations(creditTransactionTable, ({ one }) => ({
  user: one(userTable, {
    fields: [creditTransactionTable.userId],
    references: [userTable.id]
  })
}));
```

**src/app/actions/auth.ts** (Server Actions using ZSA)
```typescript
"use server";

import { createServerAction } from "zsa";
import { z } from "zod";
import { db } from "@/db";
import { userTable, passKeyCredentialTable, teamTable, teamMembershipTable, teamInvitationTable } from "@/db/schema";
import { eq, and, or, gt } from "drizzle-orm";
import { 
  createAndStoreSession, 
  getSessionFromCookie, 
  clearSession, 
  generateSessionToken,
  requireVerifiedEmail,
  canSignUp,
  getUserFromDB,
  getUserTeamsWithPermissions
} from "@/utils/auth";
import { hashPassword } from "@/utils/password-hasher";
import { generatePasskeyRegistrationOptions, verifyPasskeyRegistration } from "@/utils/webauthn";
import { sendVerificationEmail, sendTeamInvitationEmail } from "@/utils/email";
import { getIP } from "@/utils/get-IP";
import { getVerificationTokenKey, getResetTokenKey } from "@/utils/auth-utils";
import { generateSlug } from "@/utils/slugify";
import { kv } from "@vercel/kv"; // or Cloudflare KV

// Input schemas
const signInSchema = z.object({
  email: z.string().email(),
  password: z.string().min(8),
  captchaToken: z.string().optional()
});

const signUpSchema = z.object({
  email: z.string().email(),
  password: z.string().min(8),
  firstName: z.string().min(1),
  lastName: z.string().min(1),
  captchaToken: z.string().optional(),
  selectedTeam: z.string().optional()
});

const verifyEmailSchema = z.object({
  token: z.string()
});

const resetPasswordSchema = z.object({
  token: z.string(),
  password: z.string().min(8)
});

const passkeyRegistrationSchema = z.object({
  response: z.any(), // RegistrationResponseJSON
  challenge: z.string()
});

const passkeyAuthenticationSchema = z.object({
  response: z.any(), // AuthenticationResponseJSON
  challenge: z.string()
});

// Sign In Action
export const signInAction = createServerAction()
  .input(signInSchema)
  .handler(async ({ input }) => {
    const { email, password } = input;
    
    // Find user
    const user = await db.query.userTable.findFirst({
      where: eq(userTable.email, email)
    });
    
    if (!user || !user.passwordHash) {
      throw new Error("Invalid credentials");
    }
    
    // Verify password (implementation in password-hasher)
    const isValid = await verifyPassword(password, user.passwordHash);
    if (!isValid) {
      throw new Error("Invalid credentials");
    }
    
    // Create session
    await createAndStoreSession(user.id, "password");
    
    return { success: true, userId: user.id };
  });

// Sign Up Action
export const signUpAction = createServerAction()
  .input(signUpSchema)
  .handler(async ({ input }) => {
    const { email, password, firstName, lastName, selectedTeam } = input;
    const ipAddress = await getIP();
    
    // Validate signup
    await canSignUp({ email });
    
    // Hash password
    const hashedPassword = await hashPassword({ password });
    
    // Create user
    const [user] = await db.insert(userTable).values({
      email,
      firstName,
      lastName,
      passwordHash: hashedPassword,
      signUpIpAddress: ipAddress,
      emailVerified: null // Requires verification
    }).returning();
    
    // Generate verification token
    const verificationToken = generateSessionToken();
    const kv = getKV();
    await kv.put(getVerificationTokenKey(verificationToken), user.id, {
      expirationTtl: 24 * 60 * 60 // 24 hours
    });
    
    // Send verification email
    await sendVerificationEmail({
      email,
      verificationToken,
      username: `${firstName} ${lastName}`
    });
    
    // If invited to team, handle invitation acceptance
    if (selectedTeam) {
      // Handle team invitation logic
    }
    
    // Create session (but mark as unverified)
    await createAndStoreSession(user.id, "password");
    
    return { success: true, userId: user.id, requiresEmailVerification: true };
  });

// Verify Email Action
export const verifyEmailAction = createServerAction()
  .input(verifyEmailSchema)
  .handler(async ({ input }) => {
    const { token } = input;
    const kv = getKV();
    const key = getVerificationTokenKey(token);
    const userId = await kv.get(key);
    
    if (!userId) {
      throw new Error("Invalid or expired token");
    }
    
    // Update user
    await db.update(userTable)
      .set({ emailVerified: new Date() })
      .where(eq(userTable.id, userId as string));
    
    // Delete token
    await kv.delete(key);
    
    return { success: true };
  });

// Sign Out Action
export const signOutAction = createServerAction()
  .handler(async () => {
    await clearSession();
    return { success: true };
  });

// Generate Passkey Registration Options
export const generateRegistrationOptionsAction = createServerAction()
  .handler(async () => {
    const { session } = await getSessionFromCookie();
    if (!session) throw new Error("Unauthorized");
    
    const user = await getUserFromDB(session.userId);
    if (!user) throw new Error("User not found");
    
    const options = await generatePasskeyRegistrationOptions(
      user.id,
      user.email || "user"
    );
    
    return { optionsJSON: options };
  });

// Complete Passkey Registration
export const completePasskeyRegistrationAction = createServerAction()
  .input(passkeyRegistrationSchema)
  .handler(async ({ input }) => {
    const { response, challenge } = input;
    const { session } = await getSessionFromCookie();
    if (!session) throw new Error("Unauthorized");
    
    const ipAddress = await getIP();
    const headersList = headers();
    const userAgent = headersList.get("user-agent");
    
    const result = await verifyPasskeyRegistration({
      userId: session.userId,
      response,
      challenge,
      userAgent,
      ipAddress
    });
    
    return { success: result.success, credentialId: result.credential.credentialId };
  });

// Delete Passkey Action
export const deletePasskeyAction = createServerAction()
  .input(z.object({ credentialId: z.string() }))
  .handler(async ({ input }) => {
    const { credentialId } = input;
    const { session } = await getSessionFromCookie();
    if (!session) throw new Error("Unauthorized");
    
    // Verify ownership
    const passkey = await db.query.passKeyCredentialTable.findFirst({
      where: and(
        eq(passKeyCredentialTable.credentialId, credentialId),
        eq(passKeyCredentialTable.userId, session.userId)
      )
    });
    
    if (!passkey) throw new Error("Passkey not found");
    
    await db.delete(passKeyCredentialTable)
      .where(eq(passKeyCredentialTable.id, passkey.id));
    
    return { success: true };
  });

// Forgot Password Action
export const forgotPasswordAction = createServerAction()
  .input(z.object({ email: z.string().email() }))
  .handler(async ({ input }) => {
    const { email } = input;
    const user = await db.query.userTable.findFirst({
      where: eq(userTable.email, email)
    });
    
    if (user) {
      const resetToken = generateSessionToken();
      const kv = getKV();
      await kv.put(getResetTokenKey(resetToken), user.id, {
        expirationTtl: 60 * 60 // 1 hour
      });
      
      // Send reset email (implementation not shown)
    }
    
    // Always return success to prevent email enumeration
    return { success: true };
  });

// Reset Password Action
export const resetPasswordAction = createServerAction()
  .input(resetPasswordSchema)
  .handler(async ({ input }) => {
    const { token, password } = input;
    const kv = getKV();
    const key = getResetTokenKey(token);
    const userId = await kv.get(key);
    
    if (!userId) throw new Error("Invalid or expired token");
    
    const hashedPassword = await hashPassword({ password });
    
    await db.update(userTable)
      .set({ passwordHash: hashedPassword })
      .where(eq(userTable.id, userId as string));
    
    await kv.delete(key);
    
    return { success: true };
  });

// Update User Profile Action
export const updateUserProfileAction = createServerAction()
  .input(z.object({
    firstName: z.string().min(1).optional(),
    lastName: z.string().min(1).optional(),
    avatar: z.string().optional()
  }))
  .handler(async ({ input }) => {
    const { session } = await getSessionFromCookie();
    if (!session) throw new Error("Unauthorized");
    
    const updatedUser = await db.update(userTable)
      .set({ ...input, updatedAt: new Date() })
      .where(eq(userTable.id, session.userId))
      .returning();
    
    return { success: true, user: updatedUser[0] };
  });
```

### 5. Database Schema Relations (Inferred)

```typescript
// src/db/schema.ts (partial reconstruction)
import { relations } from "drizzle-orm";
import { sqliteTable, text, integer } from "drizzle-orm/sqlite-core";

export const userTable = sqliteTable("users", {
  id: text("id").primaryKey(),
  email: text("email").notNull().unique(),
  currentCredits: integer("current_credits").default(0),
  lastCreditRefreshAt: integer("last_credit_refresh_at"),
  emailVerified: integer("email_verified").default(0),
  // ... other fields
});

export const passKeyCredentialRelations = relations(userTable, ({ many }) => ({
  passkeys: many(passkeyCredentialsTable),
}));

export const teamInvitationTable = sqliteTable("team_invitations", {
  id: text("id").primaryKey(),
  email: text("email").notNull(),
  teamId: text("team_id").notNull(),
  inviterId: text("inviter_id").notNull(),
  status: text("status").default("pending"),
  // ... other fields
});

export const teamInvitationRelations = relations(teamInvitationTable, ({ one }) => ({
  team: one(teamsTable, {
    fields: [teamInvitationTable.teamId],
    references: [teamsTable.id],
  }),
  inviter: one(userTable, {
    fields: [teamInvitationTable.inviterId],
    references: [userTable.id],
  }),
}));

export const teamRelations = relations(teamsTable, ({ many }) => ({
  invitations: many(teamInvitationTable),
  members: many(teamMembersTable),
}));

export const teamRoleRelations = relations(teamMembersTable, ({ one }) => ({
  team: one(teamsTable),
  user: one(userTable),
}));
```

### 6. Email Verification Dialog Component

```tsx
// src/components/email-verification-dialog.tsx
"use client";

import { useState } from "react";
import { resendVerificationAction } from "@/app/actions/verification";
import { hasCalledVerification } from "@/lib/auth-utils"; // VOCAB_MISSING
import { Button, buttonVariants } from "@/components/ui/button";
import {
  Dialog,
  DialogContent,
  DialogHeader,
  DialogTitle,
  DialogFooter,
} from "@/components/ui/dialog";

interface EmailVerificationDialogProps {
  email: string;
  isOpen: boolean;
  onClose: () => void;
}

export function EmailVerificationDialog({
  email,
  isOpen,
  onClose,
}: EmailVerificationDialogProps) {
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);
  const [hasCalled, setHasCalled] = useState(hasCalledVerification.current);

  const handleResend = async () => {
    setIsLoading(true);
    try {
      await resendVerificationAction(email);
      hasCalledVerification.current = true;
      setHasCalled(true);
    } finally {
      setIsLoading(false);
    }
  };

  return (
    <Dialog open={isOpen} onOpenChange={onClose}>
      <DialogContent>
        <DialogHeader>
          <DialogTitle>Verify your email</DialogTitle>
        </DialogHeader>
        <p>Please verify your email address to continue.</p>
        <DialogFooter>
          <Button
            variant={buttonVariants({ variant: "outline" })}
            onClick={handleResend}
            disabled={isLoading || hasCalled}
          >
            {isLoading ? "Sending..." : "Resend verification email"}
          </Button>
        </DialogFooter>
      </DialogContent>
    </Dialog>
  );
}
```

### A) RECONSTRUCTED CODE

Based on the atlas fragments and metadata, I can reconstruct the following partial code artifacts related to the authentication and session management system:

**Session Storage Utilities (lib/session.ts or similar)**
```typescript
// KV-based session storage with TTL management
const SESSION_TTL = 60 * 60 * 24 * 7; // 7 days in seconds

// Session creation pattern observed
const createSession = async (userId: string, kv: KVNamespace) => {
  const expiresAt = new Date(Date.now() + SESSION_TTL * 1000);
  const sessionData = JSON.stringify({
    userId: user.id,
    expiresAt: expiresAt.toISOString()
  });
  
  await kv.put(`session:${userId}`, sessionData, {
    expirationTtl: Math.floor(SESSION_TTL)
  });
};

// Session retrieval pattern
const getSession = async (sessionId: string, kv: KVNamespace) => {
  const data = await kv.get(`session:${sessionId}`);
  if (!data) return null;
  return JSON.parse(data);
};
```

```typescript
// src/lib/validations/auth.ts (inferred from metadata)
import { z } from "zod";

export const signInSchema = z.object({
  email: z.string().email("Please enter a valid email address").min(1),
  password: z.string().min(1),
});

export const signUpSchema = z.object({
  email: z.string().email(),
  firstName: z.string().min(2).max(50),
  lastName: z.string().min(2).max(50),
  password: z.string().min(8),
  captchaToken: z.string(), // catchaSchema reference
});

export const forgotPasswordSchema = z.object({
  email: z.string().email(),
});

// Team creation schema (from CreateTeamForm metadata)
export const formSchema = z.object({
  name: z.string().min(1, "Team name is required").max(100),
  description: z.string().max(1000, "Description is too long").optional(),
  avatarUrl: z.string().url("Invalid URL").max(600).optional().or(z.literal("")),
});
```

### 3. Google OAuth Configuration
```typescript
// src/lib/sso/google-sso.ts (inferred)
import { Google } from "arctic";
import { isGoogleSSOEnabled } from "@/flags";

export const GOOGLE_OAUTH_STATE_COOKIE_NAME = "google_oauth_state";
export const GOOGLE_OAUTH_CODE_VERIFIER_COOKIE_NAME = "google_code_verifier";

export async function getGoogleSSOClient(): Promise<Google | null> {
  const enabled = await isGoogleSSOEnabled();
  if (!enabled) return null;
  
  return new Google(
    process.env.GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID!,
    process.env.GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET!,
    process.env.GOOGLE_REDIRECT_URI!
  );
}
```

### A) RECONSTRUCTED CODE

Based on the atlas metadata and visual patterns, the following UI components are reconstructed. These are design system primitives (likely shadcn/ui based) used in authentication flows for side panels (mobile navigation, settings sheets) and dialog headers.

**File: `src/components/ui/sheet.tsx`**

```typescript
import * as React from "react"
import * as SheetPrimitive from "@radix-ui/react-dialog"
import { cva, type VariantProps } from "class-variance-authority"
import { X } from "lucide-react"
import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"

// Base Sheet component (Radix primitive wrapper)
const Sheet = SheetPrimitive.Root

// Variant definitions for sheet positioning
const sheetVariants = cva(
  "fixed z-50 gap-4 bg-background p-6 shadow-lg transition ease-in-out " +
  "data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out " +
  "data-[state=closed]:duration-300 data-[state=open]:duration-500",
  {
    variants: {
      side: {
        top: "inset-x-0 top-0 border-b data-[state=closed]:slide-out-to-top data-[state=open]:slide-in-from-top",
        bottom: "inset-x-0 bottom-0 border-t data-[state=closed]:slide-out-to-bottom data-[state=open]:slide-in-from-bottom",
        left: "inset-y-0 left-0 h-full w-3/4 border-r data-[state=closed]:slide-out-to-left data-[state=open]:slide-in-from-left sm:max-w-sm",
        right: "inset-y-0 right-0 h-full w-3/4 border-l data-[state=closed]:slide-out-to-right data-[state=open]:slide-in-from-right sm:max-w-sm",
      },
    },
    defaultVariants: {
      side: "right",
    },
  }
)

// Extended props interface including authentication UI specific data attributes
interface SheetContentProps extends 
  React.ComponentPropsWithoutRef<typeof SheetPrimitive.Content>,
  VariantProps<typeof sheetVariants> {
  "data-sidebar"?: string
  "data-mobile"?: string
  style?: React.CSSProperties
}

// SheetContent component with forward ref and side variants
const SheetContent = React.forwardRef<
  React.ElementRef<typeof SheetPrimitive.Content>,
  SheetContentProps
>(({ 
  side = "right", 
  className, 
  "data-sidebar": dataSidebar, 
  "data-mobile": dataMobile,
  style,
  ...props 
}, ref) => (
  <SheetPrimitive.Portal>
    <SheetPrimitive.Overlay className="fixed inset-0 z-50 bg-black/80 data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:fade-out-0 data-[state=open]:fade-in-0" />
    <SheetPrimitive.Content
      ref={ref}
      className={cn(sheetVariants({ side }), className)}
      data-sidebar={dataSidebar}
      data-mobile={dataMobile}
      style={style}
      {...props}
    >
      {props.children}
      <SheetPrimitive.Close className="absolute right-4 top-4 rounded-sm opacity-70 ring-offset-background transition-opacity hover:opacity-100 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-ring focus:ring-offset-2 disabled:pointer-events-none data-[state=open]:bg-secondary">
        <X className="h-4 w-4" />
        <span className="sr-only">Close</span>
      </SheetPrimitive.Close>
    </SheetPrimitive.Content>
  </SheetPrimitive.Portal>
))
SheetContent.displayName = SheetPrimitive.Content.displayName
```

**src/app/dashboard/dashboard/billing/components/stripe-payment-form.tsx**
```typescript
"use client";

import { useStripe, useElements, PaymentElement } from "@stripe/stripe-js";
import { useState } from "react";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
import { Spinner } from "@/components/ui/spinner";

interface PaymentFormProps {
  packageId: string;
  clientSecret: string;
  onSuccess: () => void;
  onCancel: () => void;
  credits: number;
  price: number;
}

export function PaymentForm({ 
  packageId, 
  clientSecret, 
  onSuccess, 
  onCancel, 
  credits, 
  price 
}: PaymentFormProps) {
  const stripe = useStripe();
  const elements = useElements();
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);
  const [errorMessage, setErrorMessage] = useState<string>();

  const handleSubmit = async (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    if (!stripe || !elements) return;
    
    setIsLoading(true);
    setErrorMessage(undefined);

    const { error } = await stripe.confirmPayment({
      elements,
      confirmParams: {
        return_url: `${window.location.origin}/dashboard/billing/success?package_id=${packageId}`,
      },
    });

    if (error) {
      setErrorMessage(error.message);
      setIsLoading(false);
    } else {
      onSuccess();
    }
  };

  return (
    <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="space-y-4">
      <PaymentElement />
      {errorMessage && (
        <div className="text-sm text-red-500">{errorMessage}</div>
      )}
      <div className="flex gap-2 justify-end">
        <Button type="button" variant="outline" onClick={onCancel}>
          Cancel
        </Button>
        <Button type="submit" disabled={isLoading || !stripe}>
          {isLoading ? <Spinner size="sm" /> : `Pay $${price} for ${credits} credits`}
        </Button>
      </div>
    </form>
  );
}

interface StripePaymentFormProps extends PaymentFormProps {
  // Wrapper props if needed
}

export function StripePaymentForm(props: StripePaymentFormProps) {
  return <PaymentForm {...props} />;
}
```

**src/app/dashboard/dashboard/billing/components/transaction-history.tsx**
```typescript
"use client";

import { DataTable } from "@/components/data-table";
import { useState } from "react";
import { format } from "date-fns";

interface Transaction {
  id: string;
  createdAt: Date;
  credits: number;
  type: "purchase" | "usage" | "refund" | "monthly_refresh";
  description: string;
  expiresAt?: Date;
  status: "active" | "expired" | "consumed";
}

export function TransactionHistory() {
  const [pageIndex, setPageIndex] = useState(0);
  const [pageSize, setPageSize] = useState(10);

  const columns = [
    {
      accessorKey: "createdAt",
      header: "Date",
      cell: ({ row }: { row: { original: Transaction } }) => 
        format(row.original.createdAt, "MMM d, yyyy"),
    },
    {
      accessorKey: "type",
      header: "Type",
    },
    {
      accessorKey: "credits",
      header: "Credits",
    },
    {
      accessorKey: "description",
      header: "Description",
    },
    {
      accessorKey: "expiresAt",
      header: "Expires",
      cell: ({ row }: { row: { original: Transaction } }) => 
        row.original.expiresAt ? format(row.original.expiresAt, "MMM d, yyyy") : "Never",
    },
    {
      accessorKey: "status",
      header: "Status",
    },
  ];

  return (
    <div className="space-y-4">
      <h3 className="text-lg font-medium">Transaction History</h3>
      <DataTable
        columns={columns}
        data={[]}
        pageCount={0}
        pageIndex={pageIndex}
        pageSize={pageSize}
        onPageChange={setPageIndex}
        onPageSizeChange={setPageSize}
        totalCount={0}
        itemNameSingular="transaction"
        itemNamePlural="transactions"
      />
    </div>
  );
}
```

**src/components/purchase-button.tsx**
```typescript
"use client";

import { useState } from "react";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
import { useRateLimit } from "@/hooks/use-rate-limit";
import { toast } from "sonner";

interface PurchaseButtonProps {
  itemId: string;
  itemType: string;
}

export function PurchaseButton({ itemId, itemType }: PurchaseButtonProps) {
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);
  const { checkRateLimit, getRemainingTime } = useRateLimit({
    key: `purchase_${itemType}_${itemId}`,
    limit: 3,
    windowMs: 60000, // 1 minute
  });

  const handlePurchase = async () => {
    if (!checkRateLimit()) {
      const remaining = getRemainingTime();
      toast.error(`Please wait ${Math.ceil(remaining / 1000)} seconds before purchasing again`);
      return;
    }

    setIsLoading(true);
    try {
      // API call to create payment intent would go here
      const response = await fetch("/api/billing/create-payment-intent", {
        method: "POST",
        headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        body: JSON.stringify({ itemId, itemType }),
      });
      
      if (!response.ok) throw new Error("Failed to initiate purchase");
      
      const { clientSecret } = await response.json();
      // Redirect to payment or open modal
    } catch (error) {
      toast.error("Failed to initiate purchase");
    } finally {
      setIsLoading(false);
    }
  };

  return (
    <Button onClick={handlePurchase} disabled={isLoading} className="w-full">
      {isLoading ? "Processing..." : "Purchase"}
    </Button>
  );
}
```

```typescript
import { db } from "./db";
import { 
  creditTransactionTable, 
  userTable, 
  purchasedItemsTable,
  teamMembershipTable,
  teamInvitationTable,
  passKeyCredentialTable,
  projectTable,
  workflowTable
} from "./schema";
import { eq, and, desc, sql } from "drizzle-orm";

// Declaration::db.insert::CALL patterns
export async function insertCreditTransaction(data: {
  userId: string;
  amount: number;
  remainingAmount: number;
  type: string;
  description: string;
  expirationDate: Date;
  paymentIntentId: string;
}) {
  return db.insert(creditTransactionTable).values({
    userId: data.userId,
    amount: data.amount,
    remainingAmount: data.remainingAmount,
    type: data.type,
    description: data.description,
    expirationDate: data.expirationDate,
    paymentIntentId: data.paymentIntentId
  }).returning();
}

// Declaration::db.insert.values.returning::CALL
export async function insertUsageTransaction(data: {
  userId: string;
  amount: number;
  description: string;
}) {
  return db.insert(creditTransactionTable).values({
    userId: data.userId,
    amount: data.amount,
    remainingAmount: 0, // or calculated
    type: "CREDIT_TRANSACTION_TYPE.USAGE",
    description: data.description,
    createdAt: new Date(),
    updatedAt: new Date()
  }).returning();
}

// Declaration::db.update.set.where.returning::CALL
export async function updateCreditExpiration(transactionId: string, currentTime: Date) {
  return db.update(creditTransactionTable)
    .set({
      expirationDateProcessedAt: currentTime,
      remainingAmount: 0
    })
    .where(eq(creditTransactionTable.id, transactionId))
    .returning();
}

// Declaration::db.update.set::CALL
export async function updateUserCredits(userId: string, newCredits: number) {
  return db.update(userTable)
    .set({ currentCredits: newCredits })
    .where(eq(userTable.id, userId));
}

// Declaration::db.update.set.where::CALL
export async function updateUserLastRefresh(userId: string, currentTime: Date) {
  return db.update(userTable)
    .set({ lastCreditRefreshAt: currentTime })
    .where(eq(userTable.id, userId));
}

// Declaration::db.query.creditTransactionTable.findMany::CALL
export async function getUserCreditTransactions(userId: string, limit: number, offset: number) {
  return db.query.creditTransactionTable.findMany({
    where: eq(creditTransactionTable.userId, userId),
    orderBy: [desc(creditTransactionTable.createdAt)],
    limit: limit,
    offset: offset,
    columns: {
      id: true,
      amount: true,
      remainingAmount: true,
      type: true,
      description: true,
      createdAt: true,
      expirationDate: true
    }
  });
}

// Declaration::db.query.userTable.findFirst::CALL
export async function getUserWithCredits(userId: string) {
  return db.query.userTable.findFirst({
    where: eq(userTable.id, userId),
    columns: {
      id: true,
      email: true,
      currentCredits: true,
      lastCreditRefreshAt: true
    }
  });
}

// Declaration::db.select.from.where::CALL patterns
export async function selectUserTransactions(userId: string) {
  return db.select()
    .from(creditTransactionTable)
    .where(eq(creditTransactionTable.userId, userId));
}

// Declaration::db.delete.where::CALL
export async function deleteExpiredTransaction(transactionId: string) {
  return db.delete(creditTransactionTable)
    .where(eq(creditTransactionTable.id, transactionId));
}

// Declaration::db.query.teamMembershipTable.findFirst::CALL
export async function getTeamMembership(userId: string, teamId: string) {
  return db.query.teamMembershipTable.findFirst({
    where: and(
      eq(teamMembershipTable.userId, userId),
      eq(teamMembershipTable.teamId, teamId)
    )
  });
}

// Declaration::db.query.teamInvitationTable.findFirst::CALL
export async function getTeamInvitationByEmail(email: string) {
  return db.query.teamInvitationTable.findFirst({
    where: eq(teamInvitationTable.email, email)
  });
}

// Declaration::db.query.projectTable.findFirst::CALL
export async function getProjectById(projectId: string) {
  return db.query.projectTable.findFirst({
    where: eq(projectTable.id, projectId)
  });
}

// Declaration::db.query.passKeyCredentialTable.findMany::CALL
export async function getUserPassKeys(userId: string) {
  return db.query.passKeyCredentialTable.findMany({
    where: eq(passKeyCredentialTable.userId, userId)
  });
}
```

```typescript
);

);
```

```typescript
// src/lib/stripe.ts
import Stripe from 'stripe';

export function getStripe(): Stripe {
  if (!process.env.STRIPE_SECRET_KEY) {
    throw new Error('STRIPE_SECRET_KEY is not set');
  }
  return new Stripe(process.env.STRIPE_SECRET_KEY, {
    apiVersion: '2024-06-20',
  });
}
```

```typescript
import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"

  className?: string
}

  <div ref={ref} className={cn("rounded-lg border bg-card text-card-foreground shadow-sm", className)} {...props} />
))

))
```

```typescript
  }
);
FormItem.displayName = "FormItem";

const FormLabel = React.forwardRef<HTMLLabelElement, React.LabelHTMLAttributes<HTMLLabelElement>>(
  ({ className, ...props }, ref) => {
    return (
      <label ref={ref} className={cn("text-sm font-medium", className)} {...props} />
    );
  }
);
FormLabel.displayName = "FormLabel";

const FormControl = React.forwardRef<HTMLDivElement, React.HTMLAttributes<HTMLDivElement>>(
  ({ ...props }, ref) => {
    return <div ref={ref} {...props} />;
  }
);
FormControl.displayName = "FormControl";

const FormDescription = React.forwardRef<HTMLParagraphElement, React.HTMLAttributes<HTMLParagraphElement>>(
  ({ className, ...props }, ref) => {
    return (
      <p ref={ref} className={cn("text-sm text-muted-foreground", className)} {...props} />
    );
  }
);
FormDescription.displayName = "FormDescription";

const FormMessage = React.forwardRef<HTMLParagraphElement, React.HTMLAttributes<HTMLParagraphElement>>(
  ({ className, ...props }, ref) => {
    return (
      <p ref={ref} className={cn("text-sm font-medium text-destructive", className)} {...props} />
    );
  }
);
FormMessage.displayName = "FormMessage";

interface FormFieldProps {
  name: string;
  control: any;
  render: (props: { field: any }) => React.ReactNode;
  disabled?: boolean;
  defaultValue?: any;
}

function FormField({ name, control, render, disabled, defaultValue }: FormFieldProps) {
  // Implementation using react-hook-form or similar
  return (
    <FormItem>
      {render({ field: { name, value: defaultValue, onChange: () => {}, onBlur: () => {} } })}
    </FormItem>
  );
}

export { Form, FormItem, FormLabel, FormControl, FormDescription, FormMessage, FormField };
```

```typescript
// @/lib/utils.ts
import { type ClassValue, clsx } from "clsx";
import { twMerge } from "tailwind-merge";

export function cn(...inputs: ClassValue[]) {
  return twMerge(clsx(inputs));
}
```

```typescript
// @/utils/auth.ts
export function generateSessionToken(): string {
  // Generate cryptographically secure random token
  return crypto.randomUUID();
}

interface CreateKVSessionParams {
  authenticationType: "password" | "passkey" | "oauth";
  passkeyCredentialId?: string;
}

export async function createAndStoreSession(
  token: string,
  authenticationType: CreateKVSessionParams["authenticationType"],
  passkeyCredentialId?: CreateKVSessionParams["passkeyCredentialId"]
): Promise<void> {
  // Store session in KV store or database
  await fetch("/api/auth/session", {
    method: "POST",
    body: JSON.stringify({ token, authenticationType, passkeyCredentialId }),
  });
}
```

```typescript
// @/components/ui/separator.tsx
import * as React from "react";
import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";

interface SeparatorProps extends React.HTMLAttributes<HTMLDivElement> {
  orientation?: "horizontal" | "vertical";
}

export const Separator = React.forwardRef<HTMLDivElement, SeparatorProps>(
  ({ className, orientation = "horizontal", ...props }, ref) => (
    <div
      ref={ref}
      className={cn(
        "shrink-0 bg-border",
        orientation === "horizontal" ? "h-[1px] w-full" : "h-full w-[1px]",
        className
      )}
      {...props}
    />
  )
);
Separator.displayName = "Separator";
```

```typescript
// @/components/separator-with-text.tsx
import { Separator } from "@/components/ui/separator";

interface SeparatorWithTextProps {
  text: string;
  className?: string;
}

export function SeparatorWithText({ text, className }: SeparatorWithTextProps) {
  return (
    <div className={cn("relative", className)}>
      <div className="absolute inset-0 flex items-center">
        <Separator className="w-full" />
      </div>
      <div className="relative flex justify-center text-xs uppercase">
        <span className="bg-background px-2 text-muted-foreground">{text}</span>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```
